17:T20b4,# Market Pulse

Nб»Ғn tбәЈng cбәЈnh bГЎo thб»Ӣ trЖ°б»қng real-time theo mГҙ hГ¬nh B2B. Tenant Д‘Дғng kГҪ rule (ngЖ°б»Ўng giГЎ, thay Д‘б»•i %, Д‘б»ҷt biбәҝn volume), khi Д‘iб»Ғu kiб»Үn khб»ӣp hб»Ү tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng gб»Қi webhook. Dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Д‘бәҝn tб»« Binance WebSocket (~80 trades/giГўy vб»ӣi BTC/USDT).

**Mб»Ҙc Д‘Гӯch:** ДҗГўy lГ  repo mбә«u cho Lab lб»ӣn trГӘn nб»Ғn tбәЈng Praxis вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc xГўy tб»«ng bЖ°б»ӣc theo 10 chбә·ng, mб»—i chбә·ng kбәҝt thГәc bбәұng milestone cГі thб»ғ chбәЎy thбәӯt.

---

**Luб»“ng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu chГӯnh:**

```
Binance WS вҶ’ market-feed вҶ’ TradeEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ
                                            в”ңв”ҖвҶ’ aggregation вҶ’ Candle1mEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ вҶ’ rule-engine
                                            в””в”ҖвҶ’ rule-engine (khi rule match)
                                                    в”Ӯ AlertTriggeredEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ
                                                    в”ңв”ҖвҶ’ alert-delivery вҶ’ POST webhook вҶ’ tenant
                                                    в””в”ҖвҶ’ billing вҶ’ Д‘бәҝm usage вҶ’ quota check
```

---

## CбәҘu trГәc mono-repo

```
market-pulse/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ common/              # Event DTOs dГ№ng chung (duy nhбәҘt Д‘Ж°б»Јc share giб»Ҝa service)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ gateway/             # Spring Cloud Gateway вҖ” auth + routing
в”ңв”Җв”Җ identity/            # Tenant, Plan, ApiKey CRUD
в”ңв”Җв”Җ market-feed/         # Binance WS client; live/record/replay mode
в”ңв”Җв”Җ aggregation/         # Tumbling 1m window; OHLCV + VWAP
в”ңв”Җв”Җ rule-engine/         # Rule evaluation; quota check
в”ңв”Җв”Җ alert-delivery/      # Webhook delivery + DB-backed retry
в”ңв”Җв”Җ billing/             # Usage counter; quota enforcement
в”ңв”Җв”Җ dashboard/           # React + Vite SPA (NOT Gradle subproject)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ infra/               # docker-compose.yml, .env.example, RabbitMQ definitions
в”ңв”Җв”Җ docs/
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ requirements.md
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ adr/             # ADR-001 вҶ’ ADR-004
в””в”Җв”Җ README.md
```

> **Quy tбәҜc ranh giб»ӣi service:** mб»—i service chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc `implementation(project(":common"))`. KhГҙng import chГ©o giб»Ҝa cГЎc service вҖ” vi phбәЎm lГ  build error. (Xem ADR-002)

## Compose profile

Mб»—i profile nhГіm cГЎc service liГӘn quan вҖ” khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng tб»«ng phбә§n mГ  khГҙng cбә§n bбәӯt toГ n bб»ҷ JVM tб»« Chбә·ng 1.

| Profile | Service khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng | Mб»Ҙc Д‘Гӯch |
|---------|-------------------|---------|
| `core` | gateway, identity, identity-db | Auth + routing вҖ” Chбә·ng 2 |
| `feed` | market-feed, rabbitmq | DГІng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Binance вҖ” Chбә·ng 3 |
| `processing` | aggregation, aggregation-db, rule-engine, rule-engine-db, rabbitmq | Aggregation + rule eval вҖ” Chбә·ng 4вҖ“5 |
| `delivery` | alert-delivery, alert-delivery-db, billing, billing-db, mailhog, rabbitmq | Delivery + billing вҖ” Chбә·ng 6вҖ“7 |
| `full` | tбәҘt cбәЈ + dashboard | End-to-end вҖ” Chбә·ng 8вҖ“10 |

> **LЖ°u ГҪ:** CГЎc profile trГӘn sбәҪ hoГ n thiб»Үn dбә§n theo chбә·ng. б»һ Chбә·ng 1, file `docker-compose.yml` chЖ°a tб»“n tбәЎi вҖ” Д‘Ж°б»Јc build tб»« Chбә·ng 2 trб»ҹ Д‘i.

```bash
# VГӯ dб»Ҙ chбәЎy profile core (Chбә·ng 2 trб»ҹ Д‘i)
docker compose --profile core up -d

# Kiб»ғm tra health
docker compose ps

# Xem log service cб»Ҙ thб»ғ
docker compose logs -f gateway

# Dб»«ng
docker compose --profile core down
```

---

## Prerequisite

- Docker Desktop вүҘ 4.x (Engine вүҘ 24)
- Java 21 (Temurin/GraalVM CE)
- Gradle 8.x (wrapper tб»ұ tбәЈi вҖ” khГҙng cбә§n cГ i tay)
- Node.js 20+ (chб»ү cбә§n cho `dashboard/`)
- RAM tб»‘i thiб»ғu: 16 GB (profile `full` ~3.5вҖ“4.2 GB)

## Tham khбәЈo

- [docs/requirements.md](docs/requirements.md) вҖ” Product requirements
- [docs/adr/](docs/adr/) вҖ” Architecture Decision Records
- Lab content: xem trГӘn nб»Ғn tбәЈng Praxis
18:T3072,# Market Pulse вҖ” Product Requirements

> **PhбәЎm vi tГ i liб»Үu nГ y:** YГӘu cбә§u sбәЈn phбә©m Market Pulse (nб»Ғn tбәЈng B2B cбәЈnh bГЎo thб»Ӣ trЖ°б»қng).  
> YГӘu cбә§u nб»Ғn tбәЈng Lab (Praxis) khГҙng nбәұm б»ҹ Д‘Гўy.

---

## 1. VбәҘn Д‘б»Ғ cбә§n giбәЈi quyбәҝt

Doanh nghiб»Үp cбә§n theo dГөi biбәҝn Д‘б»ҷng giГЎ/volume trГӘn thб»Ӣ trЖ°б»қng tiб»Ғn mГЈ hoГЎ. GiбәЈi phГЎp hiб»Үn tбәЎi lГ  polling Д‘б»Ӣnh kб»і hoбә·c xГўy custom script вҖ” tб»‘n chi phГӯ vбәӯn hГ nh, dб»… sГіt sб»ұ kiб»Үn, khГҙng scale.

**Market Pulse** cung cбәҘp hбәЎ tбә§ng cбәЈnh bГЎo real-time theo mГҙ hГ¬nh B2B:
- Tenant Д‘Дғng kГҪ rule theo symbol + Д‘iб»Ғu kiб»Үn.
- Khi Д‘iб»Ғu kiб»Үn khб»ӣp vб»ӣi dб»Ҝ liб»Үu live (~80 trades/giГўy tб»« Binance), hб»Ү tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng gб»ӯi webhook.
- Tenant khГҙng cбә§n viбәҝt code polling, khГҙng cбә§n quбәЈn lГҪ kбәҝt nб»‘i WS, khГҙng cбә§n lo retry khi delivery thбәҘt bбәЎi.

**Chi phГӯ nбәҝu khГҙng cГі:** tб»ұ xГўy = tб»‘n kб»№ sЖ°, khГі maintain, miss nhiб»Ғu edge case (reconnect WS, retry webhook, quota enforcement).

---

## 2. Goals

| # | Outcome | Дҗo bбәұng |
|---|---------|---------|
| G1 | Hб»Ү nhбәӯn dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Binance thбәӯt vГ  xб»ӯ lГҪ real-time | `docker compose --profile full up` вҶ’ 7 JVM + DB + RabbitMQ healthy; log trade Binance Д‘бә§u tiГӘn trong 10 giГўy |
| G2 | Tenant tб»ұ quбәЈn lГҪ rule vГ  theo dГөi alert khГҙng cбә§n gб»Қi API thб»§ cГҙng | Luб»“ng tбәЎo rule вҶ’ alert trigger вҶ’ webhook DELIVERED hoГ n chб»үnh trong Dashboard |
| G3 | Hб»Ү vбәӯn hГ nh Д‘Гәng quota вҖ” vЖ°б»Јt hбәЎn mб»©c thГ¬ chбә·n rГө rГ ng, khГҙng drop silently | Rule thб»© (limit+1) вҶ’ HTTP 402; alert quota vЖ°б»Јt вҶ’ eval pause, khГҙng mбәҘt alert |
| G4 | Webhook delivery tin cбәӯy вҖ” fail tб»ұ retry, cГі audit trail Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§ | Retry 3 lбә§n (1s вҶ’ 4s вҶ’ 16s); history Д‘б»§ attempted_at + status_code + status |
| G5 | Hб»Ү phГўn tГЎch module rГө rГ ng, mб»—i service Д‘б»ҷc lбәӯp DB riГӘng | KhГҙng service nГ o query DB cб»§a service khГЎc; giao tiбәҝp chб»ү qua REST internal + RabbitMQ |

---

## 3. Non-Goals

| Дҗiб»Ғu khГҙng lГ m | LГҪ do |
|---------------|-------|
| Thanh toГЎn thбәӯt (cб»•ng payment) | Billing chб»ү cбә§n Д‘бәҝm usage + quota + xuбәҘt thГҙng tin; khГҙng tГӯch hб»Јp PSP |
| Multi-region / HA / Kubernetes | Nбәұm ngoГ i phбәЎm vi nhбәӯp mГҙn; ghi nhбәӯn Д‘б»ғ phГЎt triб»ғn sau |
| SMS delivery | Webhook + email giбәЈ lбәӯp Д‘б»§ minh hoбәЎ delivery pipeline; SMS tДғng chi phГӯ API |
| Rule phб»©c tбәЎp (AND/OR, RSI/MACD, chб»ү bГЎo kб»№ thuбәӯt) | v1 chб»ү cбә§n 3 loбәЎi rule; rule phб»©c tбәЎp lГ  lab kбәҝ thб»«a |
| Nguб»“n dб»Ҝ liб»Үu bб»• sung (BrandWatch, Wikipedia) | Adapter tГЎch bбәЎch trong `market-feed` Д‘б»ғ sau thay Binance khГҙng Д‘бәӯp lГөi вҖ” nhЖ°ng implementation Д‘б»ғ sau |

---

## 4. User Stories (Persona B вҖ” Tenant B2B)

### Rule management

- **B1 (P0):** LГ  tenant B2B, muб»‘n tбәЎo alert rule (price threshold / % change / volume spike) cho symbol quan tГўm, Д‘б»ғ hб»Ү thб»‘ng tб»ұ theo dГөi thay vГ¬ phбәЈi polling thб»§ cГҙng.
- **B2 (P0):** LГ  tenant B2B, muб»‘n nhбәӯn webhook call vб»ӣi alert payload khi rule trigger, Д‘б»ғ tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng hoГЎ hГ nh Д‘б»ҷng downstream khГҙng cбә§n polling.
- **B3 (P0):** LГ  tenant B2B, muб»‘n xem alert history vГ  delivery status (delivered / failed / retrying), Д‘б»ғ audit Д‘б»ҷ tin cбәӯy cб»§a hб»Ү.

### Usage & quota

- **B4 (P1):** LГ  tenant B2B, muб»‘n xem usage hiб»Үn tбәЎi (active rules, alerts fired this month) so vб»ӣi quota, Д‘б»ғ lГӘn kбәҝ hoбәЎch capacity.

### Edge cases

- **B5 (P0):** LГ  tenant B2B, khi webhook delivery thбәҘt bбәЎi, muб»‘n hб»Ү tб»ұ retry vб»ӣi exponential backoff, Д‘б»ғ failure tбәЎm thб»қi khГҙng Д‘б»“ng nghД©a mбәҘt alert.
- **B6 (P0):** LГ  tenant B2B, nбәҝu vЖ°б»Јt quota, muб»‘n rule evaluation pause (khГҙng drop silently), Д‘б»ғ cГі cЖЎ hб»ҷi nГўng gГіi hoбә·c giбәЈm rule thб»§ cГҙng.

---

## 5. Requirements

### P0 вҖ” Must-have

---

#### R01 вҖ” HбәЎ tбә§ng repo & Docker Compose

**MГҙ tбәЈ:** Mono-repo Gradle multi-project; 7 service Spring Boot + FE React/Vite + `infra/`.

**Docker Compose profile:**

| Profile | Service |
|---------|---------|
| `core` | gateway, identity, identity-db |
| `feed` | market-feed, rabbitmq |
| `processing` | aggregation, aggregation-db, rule-engine, rule-engine-db, rabbitmq |
| `delivery` | alert-delivery, alert-delivery-db, billing, billing-db, mailhog, rabbitmq |
| `full` | tбәҘt cбәЈ + dashboard |

**Acceptance Criteria:**
- `docker compose --profile core up -d` вҶ’ gateway :8080 + identity :8081 healthy.
- Mб»—i profile `up` khГҙng lб»—i `cannot connect to <service ngoГ i profile>`.
- Service nГ o thiбәҝu dependency ngoГ i profile вҶ’ log WARN vГ  tiбәҝp tб»Ҙc, khГҙng crash JVM.

---

#### R02 вҖ” `market-feed`: 3 chбәҝ Д‘б»ҷ hoбәЎt Д‘б»ҷng

**MГҙ tбәЈ:** Connector Binance WebSocket vб»ӣi 3 mode runtime.

| Mode | HГ nh vi |
|------|---------|
| `live` | Kбәҝt nб»‘i Binance WS public; chuбә©n hoГЎ trade вҶ’ TradeEvent; publish queue; auto-reconnect khi mбәҘt kбәҝt nб»‘i |
| `record` | Giб»‘ng `live` + ghi NDJSON ra file vб»ӣi timestamp gб»‘c |
| `replay` | Дҗб»Қc file NDJSON Д‘ГЈ record; phГЎt lбәЎi vб»ӣi multiplier Г—N; giб»Ҝ tб»ү lб»Ү thб»қi gian tЖ°ЖЎng Д‘б»‘i |

**Acceptance Criteria:**
- Chuyб»ғn mode bбәұng env `FEED_MODE=live|record|replay`.
- `replay` Г—3: phГЎt Д‘Гәng thб»© tб»ұ timestamp, hoГ n thГ nh trong 1/3 thб»қi gian gб»‘c (Вұ10%).
- `live` mбәҘt kбәҝt nб»‘i WS вҶ’ log WARN, khГҙng crash JVM, tб»ұ reconnect trong 30 giГўy.

---

#### R03 вҖ” `rule-engine`: 3 loбәЎi rule

**MГҙ tбәЈ:** Evaluate rule theo trade stream vГ  candle stream real-time.

| LoбәЎi rule | Дҗiб»Ғu kiб»Үn trigger |
|-----------|-------------------|
| `PRICE_THRESHOLD` | Symbol X vЖ°б»Јt/tб»Ҙt mб»©c giГЎ P (so vб»ӣi trade mб»ӣi nhбәҘt) |
| `PERCENT_CHANGE` | Symbol X thay Д‘б»•i вүҘ p% trong N phГәt (dГ№ng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu aggregation) |
| `VOLUME_SPIKE` | Volume 1 phГәt вүҘ kГ— trung bГ¬nh 60 phГәt (dГ№ng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu aggregation) |

**Acceptance Criteria:**
- `PRICE_THRESHOLD` kГӯch hoбәЎt trong vГІng 1 giГўy kб»ғ tб»« trade vЖ°б»Јt ngЖ°б»Ўng.
- `PERCENT_CHANGE` chГӯnh xГЎc Вұ0.1% so vб»ӣi tГӯnh tay trГӘn cГ№ng window.
- `VOLUME_SPIKE` khГҙng false-positive khi volume Д‘б»Ғu Д‘бә·n.
- Rule bб»Ӣ EVAL_PAUSED (do quota) вҶ’ khГҙng trigger, khГҙng mбәҘt dб»Ҝ liб»Үu.

---

#### R04 вҖ” `alert-delivery`: webhook + retry

**MГҙ tбәЈ:** Gб»ӯi HTTP POST Д‘бәҝn endpoint webhook cб»§a tenant khi rule trigger; xб»ӯ lГҪ retry vГ  audit.

**Payload webhook:**
```json
{
  "alertId": "uuid",
  "ruleId": "uuid",
  "symbol": "BTCUSDT",
  "ruleType": "PRICE_THRESHOLD",
  "triggeredAt": "2026-07-04T10:00:00Z",
  "triggerValue": "49850.00"
}
```

**Retry logic:**
- `2xx` вҶ’ status `DELIVERED`
- `4xx` вҶ’ status `CLIENT_ERROR`, khГҙng retry
- `5xx` / timeout вҶ’ retry sau 1s, 4s, 16s; sau 3 lбә§n вҶ’ `FAILED`

**Acceptance Criteria:**
- Alert history lЖ°u Д‘б»§: attempted_at, http_status, status mб»—i attempt.
- Sau 3 lбә§n thбәҘt bбәЎi: status = FAILED, khГҙng retry thГӘm.
- Alert vбә«n xuбәҘt hiб»Үn trong history kб»ғ cбәЈ khi FAILED.

---

#### R05 вҖ” `identity` + `gateway`: Tenant vГ  API key

**MГҙ tбәЈ:** Tenant quбәЈn lГҪ API key; gateway xГЎc thб»ұc mб»Қi request trЖ°б»ӣc khi forward.

**Auth flow:**
1. Gateway nhбәӯn `X-API-Key: <raw-key>`.
2. TГӯnh SHA-256 hash; tra cache Caffeine (TTL 5s).
3. Cache miss вҶ’ gб»Қi `identity GET /internal/keys/{hash}`.
4. Key hб»Јp lб»Ү вҶ’ thГӘm `X-Tenant-Id`, xoГЎ `X-API-Key`, forward.
5. Key khГҙng tб»“n tбәЎi / revoked вҶ’ 401.

**Acceptance Criteria:**
- Request khГҙng cГі key вҶ’ 401.
- Key sai вҶ’ 401.
- Key bб»Ӣ revoke вҶ’ 401 trong vГІng 5 giГўy (TTL cache hбәҝt).
- Request hб»Јp lб»Ү вҶ’ forward giб»Ҝ nguyГӘn body.

---

#### R06 вҖ” `billing`: usage + quota

**MГҙ tбәЈ:** Дҗбәҝm usage theo tenant; enforce quota theo gГіi.

**Quota enforcement:**
- **Rule quota (sync):** rule-engine check `billing GET /internal/quota/{tenantId}` khi tбәЎo rule; cache 30s.
- **Alert quota (async event-driven):** billing consume AlertTriggeredEvent вҶ’ Д‘бәҝm; khi vЖ°б»Јt вҶ’ phГЎt `QuotaExceededEvent` вҶ’ rule-engine pause eval tenant.

**Acceptance Criteria:**
- `usage.alertsFired` khб»ӣp Д‘бәҝm tay tб»« alert_history.
- VЖ°б»Јt quota rule вҶ’ HTTP 402 khi tбәЎo rule thб»© (limit+1); rule khГҙng Д‘Ж°б»Јc tбәЎo.
- Usage reset Д‘Гәng Д‘бә§u kб»і (thГЎng).
- VЖ°б»Јt quota alert вҶ’ rule eval pause, khГҙng drop alert Д‘ГЈ trigger trЖ°б»ӣc Д‘Гі.

---

#### R07 вҖ” `dashboard` (FE portal)

**MГҙ tбәЈ:** React + Vite SPA вҖ” giao diб»Үn quбәЈn lГҪ Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§ cho tenant.

**TГӯnh nДғng:**
- QuбәЈn lГҪ API key: tбәЎo, xem danh sГЎch, thu hб»“i.
- Rule CRUD: tбәЎo (symbol + type + params + webhookUrl), xem danh sГЎch, xoГЎ.
- Alert history: phГўn trang, filter; xem delivery attempts tб»«ng alert.
- Usage widget: active rules vs limit, alerts fired vs limit (progress bar).

**Acceptance Criteria:**
- Luб»“ng "tбәЎo rule вҶ’ thбәҘy alert trigger вҶ’ xem webhook DELIVERED" hoГ n chб»үnh trong UI, khГҙng cбә§n gб»Қi API thб»§ cГҙng.
- Dashboard hiб»ғn thб»Ӣ thГҙng bГЎo rГө khi vЖ°б»Јt quota.
- API key raw chб»ү hiб»ғn thб»Ӣ 1 lбә§n ngay sau khi tбәЎo.

---

## 6. Acceptance Criteria tб»•ng hб»Јp

### Happy path вҖ” luб»“ng end-to-end

```
Given: docker compose --profile full up -d (7 service + RabbitMQ + 5 PG + Mailhog)
  And: tenant T1 Д‘ГЈ tбәЎo, API key K1 issued
  And: rule R1 = PRICE_THRESHOLD BTC/USDT BELOW 50000
        webhook = http://localhost:9999/hook
When:  market-feed б»ҹ chбәҝ Д‘б»ҷ live
  And: BTC/USDT trade price xuб»‘ng dЖ°б»ӣi 50000
Then:  trong vГІng 2 giГўy, alert-delivery gб»ӯi POST Д‘бәҝn localhost:9999/hook
  And: payload chб»©a ruleId=R1, symbol=BTCUSDT, triggeredAt (ISO-8601), triggerValue < 50000
  And: alert history trong dashboard hiб»ғn thб»Ӣ status=DELIVERED
  And: billing tДғng alertsFired cho tenant T1 thГӘm 1
```

### Retry khi webhook fail

```
Given: endpoint webhook trбәЈ HTTP 500 liГӘn tб»Ҙc
When:  rule trigger вҶ’ alert-delivery nhбәӯn AlertTriggeredEvent
Then:  thб»ӯ lбәЎi sau 1s, thб»ӯ lбәЎi sau 4s, thб»ӯ lбәЎi sau 16s
  And: sau lбә§n thб»© 3 thбәҘt bбәЎi вҶ’ status = FAILED, khГҙng retry thГӘm
  And: alert xuбәҘt hiб»Үn trong history vб»ӣi status = FAILED vГ  attemptCount = 3
```

### Quota rule vЖ°б»Јt mб»©c

```
Given: tenant T1 cГі gГіi giб»ӣi hбәЎn 2 active rules
  And: T1 Д‘ГЈ tбәЎo 2 rule Д‘ang ACTIVE
When:  T1 gб»Қi POST /api/v1/rules Д‘б»ғ tбәЎo rule thб»© 3
Then:  gateway/rule-engine trбәЈ HTTP 402 { "error": "QUOTA_EXCEEDED_RULES" }
  And: khГҙng cГі rule nГ o Д‘Ж°б»Јc tбәЎo trong DB
  And: dashboard hiб»ғn thб»Ӣ thГҙng bГЎo vЖ°б»Јt quota
```

### Compose profile Д‘б»ҷc lбәӯp

```
Given: docker compose --profile feed up -d
When:  market-feed khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng
Then:  market-feed + rabbitmq healthy
  And: khГҙng lб»—i "cannot connect to gateway/identity/aggregation"
  And: market-feed log Д‘Ж°б»Јc Гӯt nhбәҘt 1 trade tб»« Binance WS trong 10 giГўy
```

### Replay mode

```
Given: file record cГі 1000 trade BTC/USDT ghi б»ҹ tб»‘c Д‘б»ҷ thбәӯt (T giГўy)
  And: FEED_MODE=replay, REPLAY_MULTIPLIER=3
When:  market-feed khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng chбәҝ Д‘б»ҷ replay
Then:  1000 trade phГЎt hбәҝt trong khoбәЈng T/3 giГўy (Вұ10%)
  And: thб»© tб»ұ timestamp giб»Ҝ nguyГӘn
  And: trade Д‘бә©y vГ o RabbitMQ queue giб»‘ng chбәҝ Д‘б»ҷ live
```

### Negative cases

| TГ¬nh huб»‘ng | Kбәҝt quбәЈ mong Д‘б»Јi |
|------------|-----------------|
| YAML chбә·ng khГҙng cГі field `part` | Sidenav vбә«n render, khГҙng crash |
| API key bб»Ӣ revoke | Request tiбәҝp theo trong вүӨ5s вҶ’ 401 |
| market-feed mбәҘt WS Binance | Log WARN, JVM khГҙng crash, tб»ұ reconnect |
| webhook endpoint khГҙng reach Д‘Ж°б»Јc | Timeout вҶ’ retry theo lб»Ӣch |

---

## 7. Open Questions (Д‘ГЈ giбәЈi quyбәҝt)

| # | CГўu hб»Ҹi | Quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh |
|---|---------|------------|
| OQ1 | RabbitMQ vs Kafka? | **RabbitMQ** вҖ” tiбәҝt kiб»Үm ~500MB RAM, DLQ native. (ADR-001) |
| OQ2 | Mono-repo vs multi-repo? | **Mono-repo** Gradle multi-project вҖ” 1 commit = 1 state hoГ n chб»үnh. (ADR-002) |
| OQ3 | Quota check б»ҹ Д‘Гўu? | **Hybrid**: rule CRUD = sync REST; alert quota = async event. (ADR-003) |
| OQ4 | Dashboard FE stack? | **React + Vite** вҖ” nhбәҘt quГЎn prereq. (ADR-004) |
| OQ5 | "GГЈy" Chбә·ng 9 Д‘б»Ӣnh nghД©a thбәҝ nГ o? | Queue depth > 5,000 msg VГҖ tДғng = tiГӘu chГӯ chГӯnh. (architecture В§7.1) |
19:T5bb,**ADR** (Architecture Decision Record вҖ” biГӘn bбәЈn quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh kiбәҝn trГәc) lГ  tГ i liб»Үu ngбәҜn ghi lбәЎi mб»ҷt quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh quan trб»Қng: bб»‘i cбәЈnh, cГЎc phЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn Д‘ГЈ cГўn, lб»ұa chб»Қn cuб»‘i vГ  hб»Ү quбәЈ phбәЈi chбәҘp nhбәӯn. GiГЎ trб»Ӣ cб»§a ADR nбәұm б»ҹ chб»— nГі ghi cбәЈ **lГҪ do** вҖ” 6 thГЎng sau Д‘б»Қc lбәЎi vбә«n hiб»ғu vГ¬ sao ngГ y Д‘Гі chб»Қn vбәӯy.

Hб»Ү Market Pulse cГі 4 quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh phбәЈi chб»‘t trЖ°б»ӣc khi viбәҝt dГІng code Д‘бә§u tiГӘn:

- **ADR-001 вҖ” RabbitMQ thay vГ¬ Kafka:** hб»Ү chбәЎy trГӘn laptop 16GB cГ№ng 7 JVM + 5 PostgreSQL; RabbitMQ Дғn ~150вҖ“200MB RAM cГІn Kafka cluster ngб»‘n 600вҖ“900MB. Nhu cбә§u replay Д‘ГЈ cГі б»ҹ tбә§ng market-feed nГӘn khГҙng cбә§n log bб»Ғn cб»§a Kafka.
- **ADR-002 вҖ” mono-repo Gradle multi-project:** 1 commit = 1 trбәЎng thГЎi cб»§a TOГҖN hб»Ү вҖ” Д‘Гўy lГ  xЖ°ЖЎng sб»‘ng cб»§a chГӯnh lab nГ y (bбәЎn checkout commit nГ o lГ  cГі Д‘Гәng hб»Ү б»ҹ bЖ°б»ӣc Д‘Гі). Ranh giб»ӣi service giб»Ҝ bбәұng quy Ж°б»ӣc: chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc share module common, cбәҘm import chГ©o.
- **ADR-003 вҖ” quota lai (hybrid):** CRUD rule thГ¬ hб»Ҹi billing Д‘б»“ng bб»ҷ (kГЁm cache 30s); cГІn quota alert theo hЖ°б»ӣng sб»ұ kiб»Үn вҖ” billing phГЎt QuotaExceededEvent Д‘б»ғ rule-engine tбәЎm dб»«ng Д‘ГЎnh giГЎ. Gateway KHГ”NG check quota.
- **ADR-004 вҖ” dashboard React + Vite:** tГЎi dГ№ng Д‘Гәng stack FE Д‘ГЈ hб»Қc б»ҹ Lab Mini-Wiki, khГҙng thГӘm cГҙng nghб»Ү mб»ӣi khГҙng cбә§n thiбәҝt.
1a:T1328,# ADR-001 вҖ” Message Queue: chб»Қn RabbitMQ thay vГ¬ Kafka

| TrЖ°б»қng | GiГЎ trб»Ӣ |
|--------|---------|
| **Status** | Accepted |
| **NgГ y quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh** | 2026-07-05 |
| **NgЖ°б»қi quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh** | Architect (Market Pulse GДҗ1) |
| **Blocking** | GДҗ2 вҖ” tбәҘt cбәЈ service khГҙng implement queue trЖ°б»ӣc khi ADR nГ y chб»‘t |

---

## Context

Hб»Ү Market Pulse cбә§n mб»ҷt message broker (phбә§n mб»Ғm trung gian nhбәӯn vГ  phГўn phб»‘i message giб»Ҝa cГЎc service) Д‘б»ғ:

1. **Fanout trade stream** вҖ” 1 nguб»“n (`market-feed`) вҶ’ nhiб»Ғu consumer (`aggregation`, `rule-engine`).
2. **Async delivery pipeline** вҖ” `rule-engine` вҶ’ `alert-delivery` + `billing` mГ  khГҙng gб»Қi trб»ұc tiбәҝp.
3. **Retry / dead-letter** вҖ” `alert-delivery` cбә§n cЖЎ chбәҝ xб»ӯ lГҪ message thбәҘt bбәЎi.

**RГ ng buб»ҷc cб»©ng:** Lab chбәЎy trГӘn laptop cГЎ nhГўn (16 GB RAM) cГ№ng 7 JVM + 5 PostgreSQL + broker. Tб»•ng RAM phбәЈi вүӨ ~4.5 GB Д‘б»ғ thoбәЈi mГЎi вҖ” khГҙng bao gб»“m OS + browser.

---

## CГЎc lб»ұa chб»Қn

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn A вҖ” Apache Kafka 3.7 (KRaft mode)

**Kafka** lГ  distributed streaming platform (nб»Ғn tбәЈng stream phГўn tГЎn) вҖ” dб»Ҝ liб»Үu lЖ°u dбәЎng log, consumer Д‘б»Қc theo offset, cГі thб»ғ replay tб»« bбәҘt kб»і Д‘iб»ғm nГ o.

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| Adoption | ~500M Docker Hub pulls (confluent/kafka) |
| RAM broker | ~600вҖ“900 MB (KRaft mode, khГҙng ZooKeeper) |
| RAM tб»•ng (7 JVM + 5 PG + broker) | ~4.5вҖ“5.0 GB вҖ” sГЎt hoбә·c vЖ°б»Јt ngЖ°б»Ўng |
| Retry / Dead-letter queue (DLQ) | KhГҙng native вҖ” tб»ұ implement bбәұng topic riГӘng |
| Topic/partition setup | Trung bГ¬nh: tбәЎo topic + partition trЖ°б»ӣc khi chбәЎy |
| Replay dб»Ҝ liб»Үu thб»Ӣ trЖ°б»қng | Built-in (consumer offset reset) |
| Spring support | `spring-kafka` 9 nДғm; production-proven |
| Learning value | Cao nhбәҘt cho distributed systems |

**Trade-off:** RAM quГЎ lб»ӣn cho lab laptop; DLQ phбәЈi tб»ұ implement tДғng Д‘б»ҷ phб»©c tбәЎp.

---

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn B вҖ” RabbitMQ 3.13

**RabbitMQ** lГ  message broker truyб»Ғn thб»‘ng (broker trung gian nhбәӯn/gб»ӯi message) вҖ” model push-based, hб»— trб»Ј nhiб»Ғu loбәЎi exchange (fanout, topic, direct, headers).

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| Adoption | Docker Hub 1B+ pulls |
| RAM broker | ~150вҖ“200 MB |
| RAM tб»•ng (7 JVM + 5 PG + broker) | ~3.7вҖ“4.2 GB вң“ |
| Retry / Dead-letter queue (DLQ) | **Native** вҖ” `x-dead-letter-exchange`, `x-message-ttl` |
| Setup | ThбәҘp: 1 container, Management UI :15672 cГі sбәөn |
| Replay built-in | KhГҙng вҖ” nhЖ°ng `market-feed replay mode` thay thбәҝ |
| Spring support | `spring-boot-starter-amqp` 14 nДғm; battle-tested |
| Learning value | Tб»‘t cho pattern queue/exchange; thiбәҝu offset/partition |

---

### So sГЎnh tб»•ng hб»Јp

| TiГӘu chГӯ | RabbitMQ | Kafka |
|----------|----------|-------|
| RAM broker | **~175 MB** | ~750 MB |
| RAM tiбәҝt kiб»Үm | вҖ” | tб»‘n thГӘm ~575 MB |
| PhГ№ hб»Јp RAM 16 GB laptop | вң“ ThoбәЈi mГЎi | вҡ  SГЎt ngЖ°б»Ўng |
| DLQ / retry native | вң“ | вң— |
| Replay dб»Ҝ liб»Үu thб»Ӣ trЖ°б»қng | Qua `market-feed` | Built-in |
| Дҗб»ҷ phб»©c tбәЎp setup | ThбәҘp | Trung bГ¬nh |
| Spring maturity | 14 nДғm | 9 nДғm |

---

## Quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh

**Chб»Қn RabbitMQ 3.13.**

LГҪ do quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh:

1. **RAM lГ  rГ ng buб»ҷc cб»©ng** вҖ” tiбәҝt kiб»Үm ~500вҖ“575 MB so vб»ӣi Kafka; profile `full` vГ o khoбәЈng 3.7вҖ“4.2 GB thay vГ¬ 4.5вҖ“5.0 GB. Vб»ӣi laptop 16 GB chбәЎy OS + browser + Docker, khoбәЈng cГЎch nГ y quan trб»Қng.

2. **DLQ native** вҖ” pattern retry/dead-letter cб»§a `alert-delivery` implement trб»ұc tiбәҝp bбәұng `x-dead-letter-exchange`, khГҙng phбәЈi tб»ұ viбәҝt logic.

3. **Replay dб»Ҝ liб»Үu** вҖ” `market-feed replay mode` (Д‘б»Қc NDJSON, phГЎt lбәЎi theo multiplier) Д‘ГЎp б»©ng hoГ n toГ n nhu cбә§u lab mГ  khГҙng cбә§n broker replay.

4. **TбәҘt cбәЈ pattern cбә§n dбәЎy Д‘б»Ғu implement Д‘Ж°б»Јc:** async messaging, fanout, topic routing, multiple consumer, retry/DLQ.

---

## Consequences

**TГӯch cб»ұc:**
- ToГ n bб»ҷ pattern dбәЎy trong Lab Д‘б»Ғu cover: fanout exchange, topic routing, direct delivery, retry + DLQ.
- Management UI :15672 lГ  cГҙng cб»Ҙ quan sГЎt trб»ұc quan cho Chбә·ng 9 (queue depth, message rate).
- Replay dб»Ҝ liб»Үu thб»Ӣ trЖ°б»қng giбәЈi quyбәҝt б»ҹ tбә§ng `market-feed` вҖ” tГЎch bбәЎch hЖЎn.

**ДҗГЎnh Д‘б»•i / hбәЎn chбәҝ:**
- KhГҙng dбәЎy Д‘Ж°б»Јc consumer group offset, partition, log retention вҖ” cГЎc concept cб»‘t lГөi cб»§a Kafka.
- Lab ghi nhбәӯn rГө: **"Khi nГ o cбә§n Kafka"** вҖ” khi cбә§n: (a) nhiб»Ғu consumer group Д‘б»ҷc lбәӯp replay tб»« Д‘бә§u, (b) retention dб»Ҝ liб»Үu dГ i hбәЎn, (c) throughput > 100k msg/s. Market Pulse khГҙng Д‘ГЎp б»©ng Д‘iб»Ғu kiб»Үn nГ o trong sб»‘ nГ y.
- Nбәҝu sau nГ y scale lГӘn Kafka, phбәЈi thay toГ n bб»ҷ `spring-amqp` bбәұng `spring-kafka` вҖ” khГҙng drop-in.
1b:T1613,# ADR-002 вҖ” CбәҘu trГәc repo: Mono-repo Gradle multi-project

| TrЖ°б»қng | GiГЎ trб»Ӣ |
|--------|---------|
| **Status** | Accepted |
| **NgГ y quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh** | 2026-07-05 |
| **NgЖ°б»қi quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh** | Architect (Market Pulse GДҗ1) |
| **Blocking** | GДҗ2 вҖ” cбәҘu trГәc repo phбәЈi chб»‘t trЖ°б»ӣc khi DEV bбәҜt Д‘бә§u bбәҘt kб»і service nГ o |

---

## Context

Market Pulse gб»“m 7 service Spring Boot + 1 FE + infra. Cбә§n quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh chб»©a tбәҘt cбәЈ trong 1 repo (mono-repo) hay tГЎch ra tб»«ng repo riГӘng (multi-repo).

**RГ ng buб»ҷc Д‘бә·c thГ№ cб»§a Lab:** Mб»—i bЖ°б»ӣc trong 10 chбә·ng cбә§n mб»ҷt `commit_ref` вҖ” con trб»Ҹ Д‘бәҝn commit mбә«u Д‘б»ғ ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc diff khi bб»Ӣ kбә№t. ДҗГўy lГ  xЖ°ЖЎng sб»‘ng cб»§a Lab, бәЈnh hЖ°б»ҹng trб»ұc tiбәҝp Д‘бәҝn lб»ұa chб»Қn cбәҘu trГәc repo.

---

## CГЎc lб»ұa chб»Қn

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn A вҖ” Multi-repo (8 repo riГӘng biб»Үt)

Mб»—i service lГ  1 repository GitHub Д‘б»ҷc lбәӯp. `dashboard/` vГ  `infra/` thГӘm 2 repo nб»Ҝa.

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| Clone | 8 lб»Үnh `git clone` hoбә·c 1 repo tб»•ng dГ№ng submodule |
| Docker Compose | PhбәЈi bind-mount tб»« nhiб»Ғu thЖ° mб»Ҙc khГЎc nhau |
| Commit-per-step | 1 bЖ°б»ӣc Lab = cбәӯp nhбәӯt 1вҖ“3 repo вҶ’ nhiб»Ғu commit ID, khГі Д‘б»‘i chiбәҝu |
| Ranh giб»ӣi service | Physical enforce вҖ” khГҙng thб»ғ import chГ©o vб»Ғ mбә·t file system |
| CI/CD | Trigger riГӘng per repo; phб»©c tбәЎp khi thay Д‘б»•i cross-service |
| Onboarding | NgЖ°б»қi hб»Қc cбә§n clone nhiб»Ғu repo trЖ°б»ӣc khi bбәҜt Д‘бә§u bЖ°б»ӣc Д‘бә§u tiГӘn |

**HбәЎn chбәҝ chГӯnh:** `commit_ref` trбәЈi rбәЈi 8 repo вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc phбәЈi tra nhiб»Ғu nЖЎi khi stuck.

---

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn B вҖ” Mono-repo, Gradle multi-project

Mб»ҷt repo duy nhбәҘt; mб»—i service lГ  Gradle subproject (`:gateway`, `:identity`, ...). `dashboard/` lГ  thЖ° mб»Ҙc Node riГӘng, khГҙng phбәЈi Gradle subproject.

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| Clone | 1 lб»Үnh `git clone` |
| Docker Compose | `infra/docker-compose.yml` tham chiбәҝu context tЖ°ЖЎng Д‘б»‘i вҖ” tб»ұ nhiГӘn |
| Commit-per-step | **1 commit ID = toГ n bб»ҷ trбәЎng thГЎi hб»Ү** вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc `git checkout <hash>` lГ  Д‘б»§ |
| Ranh giб»ӣi service | Enforce bбәұng quy Ж°б»ӣc Gradle: `common/` duy nhбәҘt Д‘Ж°б»Јc share; service khГЎc khГҙng import chГ©o |
| CI/CD | 1 pipeline, filter path Д‘б»ғ build chб»ү service thay Д‘б»•i |
| Onboarding | 1 lб»Үnh, 1 IDE window |

**Tham chiбәҝu:** `spring-projects/spring-petclinic-microservices` (5.2k вӯҗ) dГ№ng cГ№ng pattern.

---

### So sГЎnh tб»•ng hб»Јp

| TiГӘu chГӯ | Mono-repo | Multi-repo |
|----------|-----------|------------|
| commit_ref cho Lab | вң“ 1 hash = 1 state hoГ n chб»үnh | вң— TrбәЈi rбәЈi N repo |
| Onboarding | вң“ 1 lб»Үnh | вң— N lб»Үnh |
| Docker Compose | вң“ Tб»ұ nhiГӘn | вң— Phб»©c tбәЎp bind-mount |
| Ranh giб»ӣi service | Convention (enforce Д‘Ж°б»Јc qua Gradle config) | Physical |
| Scale vб»Ғ sau | CГі thб»ғ extract khi thбәӯt sб»ұ cбә§n | Tб»« Д‘бә§u Д‘ГЈ tГЎch |

---

## Quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh

**Chб»Қn mono-repo, Gradle multi-project.**

LГҪ do:

1. **`commit_ref` lГ  xЖ°ЖЎng sб»‘ng Lab** вҖ” chб»ү mono-repo cho phГ©p 1 commit ID map Д‘бәҝn trбәЎng thГЎi Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§ cб»§a tбәҘt cбәЈ service. ДҗГўy lГ  tГӯnh nДғng khГҙng thб»ғ Д‘ГЎnh Д‘б»•i.

2. **Onboarding tб»‘i thiб»ғu** вҖ” 1 `git clone`, mб»ҹ 1 IDE window, chбәЎy 1 `docker compose`.

3. **Ranh giб»ӣi service** vбә«n enforce Д‘Ж°б»Јc bбәұng quy tбәҜc Gradle вҖ” mбәЎnh hЖЎn quy Ж°б»ӣc vДғn bбәЈn.

---

## CбәҘu trГәc thЖ° mб»Ҙc

```
market-pulse/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ common/          # Event DTOs вҖ” duy nhбәҘt Д‘Ж°б»Јc share giб»Ҝa service
в”ңв”Җв”Җ gateway/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ identity/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ market-feed/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ aggregation/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ rule-engine/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ alert-delivery/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ billing/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ dashboard/       # React/Vite вҖ” KHГ”NG phбәЈi Gradle subproject
в”ңв”Җв”Җ infra/
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ docker-compose.yml
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ .env.example
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ rabbitmq/
в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җ definitions.json
в””в”Җв”Җ docs/
```

**`settings.gradle.kts` khai bГЎo:**
```kotlin
include(":common", ":gateway", ":identity", ":market-feed",
        ":aggregation", ":rule-engine", ":alert-delivery", ":billing")
// dashboard/ khГҙng include вҖ” dГ№ng npm, khГҙng Gradle
```

---

## Quy tбәҜc ranh giб»ӣi service (enforcement)

Mб»—i service chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc khai bГЎo:
```kotlin
// OK
dependencies {
    implementation(project(":common"))
}

// KHГ”NG Д‘Ж°б»Јc phГ©p
dependencies {
    implementation(project(":identity"))   // cross-service import вҖ” build error
}
```

`common/` chб»ү chб»©a Event DTOs (dГ№ng trong messaging) vГ  cГЎc shared value object thuбә§n (khГҙng Spring bean, khГҙng repository). Giao tiбәҝp giб»Ҝa service: REST internal (sync) hoбә·c RabbitMQ (async) вҖ” khГҙng bao giб»қ gб»Қi trб»ұc tiбәҝp method Java.

---

## Consequences

**TГӯch cб»ұc:**
- NgЖ°б»қi hб»Қc bбәҜt Д‘бә§u vб»ӣi 1 lб»Үnh clone, 1 IDE, 1 compose file.
- `git log --oneline` cб»§a Lab Д‘б»Қc nhЖ° changelog cГі cбәҘu trГәc.
- CI/CD Д‘ЖЎn giбәЈn hЖЎn ban Д‘бә§u; extract service ra repo riГӘng lГ  bЖ°б»ӣc tб»ұ nhiГӘn khi scale.

**ДҗГЎnh Д‘б»•i / hбәЎn chбәҝ:**
- Mono-repo lГ m mб»қ Д‘i tГӯnh "hoГ n toГ n Д‘б»ҷc lбәӯp" cб»§a tб»«ng service вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc phбәЈi tб»ұ kб»· luбәӯt khГҙng import chГ©o.
- Khi repo lб»ӣn, `git clone` tбәЈi vб»Ғ toГ n bб»ҷ history cб»§a tбәҘt cбәЈ service (giбәЈm nhбә№ bбәұng `--depth 1` hoбә·c sparse checkout sau nГ y).
- Nбәҝu sau nГ y muб»‘n deploy service riГӘng lбә» lГӘn K8s vб»ӣi CI/CD per-service, cбә§n thГӘm cбәҘu hГ¬nh path filter вҖ” khГҙng cбә§n bГўy giб»қ.
1c:T1983,# ADR-003 вҖ” Quota check: chiбәҝn lЖ°б»Јc Hybrid (sync + event-driven)

| TrЖ°б»қng | GiГЎ trб»Ӣ |
|--------|---------|
| **Status** | Accepted |
| **NgГ y quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh** | 2026-07-05 |
| **NgЖ°б»қi quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh** | Architect (Market Pulse GДҗ1) |
| **Blocking** | GДҗ2-Ch2 вҖ” thiбәҝt kбәҝ gateway + billing phб»Ҙ thuб»ҷc quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh nГ y |

---

## Context

Market Pulse cГі 2 loбәЎi quota cбә§n enforce:

1. **Quota rule:** Tenant chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc tбәЎo tб»‘i Д‘a N rule active (theo gГіi).
2. **Quota alert:** Tenant chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc bбәҜn tб»‘i Д‘a M alert/thГЎng.

Cбә§n quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh **Д‘бә·t logic check quota б»ҹ Д‘Гўu** vГ  **dГ№ng cЖЎ chбәҝ Д‘б»“ng bб»ҷ hay bбәҘt Д‘б»“ng bб»ҷ**.

**Bб»‘i cбәЈnh:** `gateway` (Spring Cloud Gateway вҖ” WebFlux reactive) xб»ӯ lГҪ mб»Қi request Д‘бәҝn. `billing` lЖ°u trб»Ҝ usage counter. `rule-engine` tбәЎo rule vГ  evaluate chГәng.

---

## CГЎc lб»ұa chб»Қn

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn A вҖ” Gateway check quota cho mб»Қi request

Gateway hб»Ҹi `billing` mб»—i khi cГі request tбәЎo rule / mб»—i khi alert trigger вҖ” trЖ°б»ӣc khi forward.

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| Latency | Mб»—i request thГӘm 1 REST call Д‘бәҝn billing (thЖ°б»қng ~5вҖ“10ms trong Docker network) |
| Coupling | Gateway phбәЈi biбәҝt vб»Ғ quota logic cб»§a tб»«ng business operation вҖ” vi phбәЎm SRP |
| Consistency | Strong вҖ” quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh luГҙn dб»ұa trГӘn data mб»ӣi nhбәҘt |
| Scaling | Gateway trб»ҹ thГ nh bottleneck nбәҝu billing chбәӯm; phбәЈi cache hoбә·c timeout xб»ӯ lГҪ phб»©c tбәЎp |

**HбәЎn chбәҝ chГӯnh:** Gateway nГӘn stateless vГ  chб»ү lo auth + routing. NhГәng quota logic vГ o Gateway lГ m phГ¬nh trГЎch nhiб»Үm vГ  tбәЎo tight coupling vб»ӣi billing schema.

---

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn B вҖ” Rule-engine check quota khi tбәЎo rule (sync); Alert quota hoГ n toГ n sync

Rule-engine gб»Қi billing mб»—i khi tenant tбәЎo rule. Alert quota cЕ©ng check Д‘б»“ng bб»ҷ trЖ°б»ӣc khi evaluate.

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| Rule create latency | +10вҖ“15ms (1 REST call trong Docker network) вҖ” chбәҘp nhбәӯn Д‘Ж°б»Јc cho CRUD |
| Alert hot path | Check Д‘б»“ng bб»ҷ trЖ°б»ӣc mб»—i TradeEvent вҶ’ tДғng latency evaluation Д‘ГЎng kб»ғ |
| Consistency | Strong cho cбәЈ hai |
| Complexity | Alert-delivery vГ  billing phбәЈi sync trЖ°б»ӣc khi eval вҖ” tбәЎo tight coupling trГӘn hot path |

**HбәЎn chбәҝ chГӯnh:** TradeEvent Д‘бәҝn 80/giГўy вҖ” check quota Д‘б»“ng bб»ҷ trЖ°б»ӣc mб»—i eval = bottleneck trб»ұc tiбәҝp trГӘn hot path.

---

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn C вҖ” Hybrid: Rule quota sync + Alert quota event-driven вң“

- **Rule quota** (P0, cold path): rule-engine gб»Қi `billing GET /internal/quota/{tenantId}` khi CREATE rule; cache Caffeine 30s; nбәҝu `rulesQuotaExceeded=true` вҶ’ trбәЈ 402.
- **Alert quota** (P0, hot path): billing consume `AlertTriggeredEvent` вҶ’ Д‘бәҝm usage вҶ’ khi vЖ°б»Јt вҶ’ phГЎt `QuotaExceededEvent` вҶ’ rule-engine nhбәӯn вҶ’ Д‘ГЎnh dбәҘu tenant `EVAL_PAUSED` вҶ’ ngб»«ng evaluate rule cб»§a tenant Д‘Гі.
- **Gateway** khГҙng check quota вҖ” chб»ү auth.

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| Rule create latency | +10ms (1 REST call) вҖ” OK cho CRUD |
| Alert hot path latency | KhГҙng bб»Ӣ chбә·n вҖ” hot path khГҙng chб»қ billing |
| Consistency | Rule: strong (30s cache); Alert: eventual ~1s |
| Coupling | Gateway stateless; rule-engine biбәҝt vб»Ғ quota state qua event вҖ” loose coupling |
| Complexity | Rule-engine cбә§n in-memory quota state + warm lбәЎi khi restart |

---

### So sГЎnh tб»•ng hб»Јp

| TiГӘu chГӯ | A: Gateway check | B: Rule-engine sync | C: Hybrid вң“ |
|----------|-----------------|---------------------|-------------|
| Gateway stateless | вң— | вң“ | вң“ |
| Hot path khГҙng bб»Ӣ block | вң— | вң— | вң“ |
| Rule quota consistency | Strong | Strong | Strong (30s) |
| Alert quota consistency | Strong | Strong | Eventual (~1s) |
| Дҗб»ҷ phб»©c tбәЎp | Trung bГ¬nh | Cao | Trung bГ¬nh |

---

## Quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh

**Chб»Қn PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn C вҖ” Hybrid.**

LГҪ do:

1. **Gateway giб»Ҝ stateless** вҖ” chб»ү auth (SHA-256 + cache) + routing. KhГҙng phбәЈi biбәҝt vб»Ғ quota.

2. **Rule quota lГ  cold path** вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi dГ№ng tбәЎo rule khГҙng thЖ°б»қng xuyГӘn; +10ms cho 1 REST call chбәҘp nhбәӯn Д‘Ж°б»Јc; `rulesQuotaExceeded` khГҙng thay Д‘б»•i liГӘn tб»Ҙc.

3. **Alert quota lГ  hot path** вҖ” 80 trades/giГўy, mб»—i trade Д‘i qua rule evaluation; blocking sync check = bottleneck. Event-driven cho phГ©p hot path chбәЎy khГҙng bб»Ӣ chбә·n; khi billing phГЎt `QuotaExceededEvent`, rule-engine nhбәӯn vГ  pause вҖ” eventual consistency ~1s Д‘б»§ cho usecase nГ y.

---

## Chi tiбәҝt implementation

### Rule quota (sync)

```
POST /api/v1/rules
  вҶ’ rule-engine: check in-memory quota cache
  вҶ’ cache miss (hoбә·c hбәҝt 30s TTL): GET billing /internal/quota/{tenantId}
  вҶ’ rulesQuotaExceeded = true вҶ’ HTTP 402 { "error": "QUOTA_EXCEEDED_RULES" }
  вҶ’ false вҶ’ tбәЎo rule вҶ’ cache invalidate
```

Caffeine cache key: `tenantId`; TTL: 30s; evict khi rule CRUD thay Д‘б»•i count.

### Alert quota (event-driven)

```
AlertTriggeredEvent вҶ’ billing (consume)
  вҶ’ INSERT/UPDATE usage_periods.alerts_fired++
  вҶ’ IF alerts_fired > plan.max_alerts_pm:
      publish QuotaExceededEvent { tenantId, quotaType="ALERTS", ... }

QuotaExceededEvent вҶ’ rule-engine (consume)
  вҶ’ SET tenant.alertsQuotaExceeded = true (in-memory map)
  вҶ’ evaluate(): nбәҝu tenant bб»Ӣ flag вҶ’ skip, khГҙng publish AlertTriggeredEvent
```

Rule-engine warm lбәЎi quota state khi restart: gб»Қi `billing GET /internal/quota/{tenantId}` cho tбәҘt cбәЈ tenant cГі rule ACTIVE.

---

## Consequences

**TГӯch cб»ұc:**
- Hot path (trade вҶ’ eval вҶ’ alert) khГҙng bб»Ӣ blocking quota check.
- Gateway stateless вҖ” dб»… scale horizontal nбәҝu cбә§n.
- PhГўn tГЎch rГө: rule-engine biбәҝt vб»Ғ quota state, gateway khГҙng biбәҝt gГ¬ vб»Ғ business quota.

**ДҗГЎnh Д‘б»•i / hбәЎn chбәҝ:**
- **Eventual consistency ~1s** cho alert quota: trong khoбәЈnh khбәҜc vЖ°б»Јt quota, cГі thб»ғ thГӘm vГ i alert Д‘Ж°б»Јc bбәҜn trЖ°б»ӣc khi `QuotaExceededEvent` Д‘Ж°б»Јc xб»ӯ lГҪ. ChбәҘp nhбәӯn Д‘Ж°б»Јc вҖ” khГҙng cГі tГ¬nh huб»‘ng nГ o trong Lab yГӘu cбә§u hard real-time quota enforcement trГӘn hot path.
- **In-memory quota state** trong rule-engine cбә§n warm lбәЎi khi restart вҖ” thГӘm startup dependency vб»ӣi `billing`.
- Nбәҝu billing service down: rule-engine dГ№ng cached state (stale tб»‘i Д‘a 30s cho rule quota); alert quota enforcement bб»Ӣ delay cho Д‘бәҝn khi billing back online.
1d:T1537,# ADR-004 вҖ” Dashboard Frontend: React + Vite

| TrЖ°б»қng | GiГЎ trб»Ӣ |
|--------|---------|
| **Status** | Accepted |
| **NgГ y quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh** | 2026-07-05 |
| **NgЖ°б»қi quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh** | PO + Architect (Market Pulse GДҗ1) |
| **Blocking** | Non-blocking (cГі thб»ғ quyбәҝt sau OQ1вҖ“3; tuy nhiГӘn бәЈnh hЖ°б»ҹng cбәҘu hГ¬nh CORS gateway) |

---

## Context

Market Pulse cбә§n mб»ҷt giao diб»Үn web cho tenant Д‘б»ғ quбәЈn lГҪ API key, rule CRUD, xem alert history vГ  usage widget.

**Ngб»Ҝ cбәЈnh Lab:** NgЖ°б»қi hб»Қc Д‘ГЈ lГ m qua mini-wiki vб»ӣi React + Vite. ДҗГўy lГ  prereq (Д‘iб»Ғu kiб»Үn tiГӘn quyбәҝt) cб»§a Lab lб»ӣn Market Pulse. Thay Д‘б»•i stack FE = tДғng thГӘm learning curve khГҙng liГӘn quan Д‘бәҝn mб»Ҙc tiГӘu chГӯnh (hiб»ғu kiбәҝn trГәc microservices, khГҙng phбәЈi hб»Қc FE mб»ӣi).

---

## CГЎc lб»ұa chб»Қn

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn A вҖ” React + Vite (giб»Ҝ nguyГӘn prereq) вң“

**React** (95M npm downloads/tuбә§n) вҖ” UI library dб»ұa trГӘn component.  
**Vite** (70k вӯҗ GitHub) вҖ” build tool thбәҝ hб»Ү mб»ӣi dГ№ng ES modules native; dev server cold start < 300ms.

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| NhбәҘt quГЎn prereq | вң“ NgЖ°б»қi hб»Қc Д‘ГЈ quen tб»« mini-wiki |
| Time-to-first-screen (dev) | Nhanh вҖ” Vite HMR (Hot Module Replacement) instant |
| PhГ№ hб»Јp use case | вң“ SPA (Single-Page Application) вҖ” dashboard CRUD authenticated khГҙng cбә§n SSR |
| Tooling ecosystem | Vite + React Router + Tanstack Query вҖ” stable, docs tб»‘t |
| Дҗб»ҷ phб»©c tбәЎp setup | ThбәҘp вҖ” `npm create vite@latest` lГ  Д‘б»§ |
| Adoption | React: Facebook, Airbnb, Netflix; Vite: Vue official, Svelte |

---

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn B вҖ” Next.js (React vб»ӣi SSR/SSG)

**Next.js** (127k вӯҗ GitHub, 7M npm downloads/tuбә§n) вҖ” React framework thГӘm SSR (Server-Side Rendering), file-based routing, API routes.

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| NhбәҘt quГЎn prereq | вң— NgЖ°б»қi hб»Қc chЖ°a biбәҝt Next.js routing, App Router, server component |
| PhГ№ hб»Јp use case | SSR/SSG khГҙng cбә§n thiбәҝt cho dashboard nб»ҷi bб»ҷ sau auth |
| Complexity | Cao hЖЎn: hydration, server component, route group, middleware |
| GiГЎ trб»Ӣ thГӘm | DбәЎy Next.js nhЖ°ng Д‘Гўy khГҙng phбәЈi mб»Ҙc tiГӘu Lab |

---

### PhЖ°ЖЎng ГЎn C вҖ” Vue 3 + Vite

| TiГӘu chГӯ | ДҗГЎnh giГЎ |
|----------|----------|
| NhбәҘt quГЎn prereq | вң— NgЖ°б»қi hб»Қc biбәҝt React, khГҙng biбәҝt Vue Composition API |
| ChбәҘt lЖ°б»Јng | Tб»‘t вҖ” Vue 3 mature, Vite lГ  official build tool |
| Barrier | Дҗб»•i syntax (script setup, ref, reactive, v-if/v-for) |
| GiГЎ trб»Ӣ thГӘm | DбәЎy Vue nhЖ°ng Д‘Гўy khГҙng phбәЈi mб»Ҙc tiГӘu Lab |

---

### So sГЎnh tб»•ng hб»Јp

| TiГӘu chГӯ | React + Vite вң“ | Next.js | Vue 3 + Vite |
|----------|----------------|---------|--------------|
| Prereq nhбәҘt quГЎn | вң“ | Gбә§n (React nhЖ°ng thГӘm framework) | вң— |
| PhГ№ hб»Јp SPA dashboard | вң“ | Overkill | вң“ |
| Learning curve thГӘm | KhГҙng | Trung bГ¬nh | Cao |
| Ecosystem | Mature | Mature | Mature |

---

## Quyбәҝt Д‘б»Ӣnh

**Chб»Қn React + Vite.**

LГҪ do:

1. **NhбәҘt quГЎn prereq** вҖ” khГҙng Д‘б»•i stack FE Д‘б»“ng nghД©a ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc tбәӯp trung vГ o mб»Ҙc tiГӘu chГӯnh: hiб»ғu kiбәҝn trГәc microservices, khГҙng phбәЈi hб»Қc framework mб»ӣi.

2. **SPA Д‘б»§ dГ№ng** вҖ” dashboard lГ  authenticated CRUD portal; khГҙng cГі URL cГҙng khai cбә§n index; khГҙng cбә§n SEO; SSR mang lбәЎi zero benefit.

3. **Dev experience tб»‘t** вҖ” Vite HMR nhanh; build nhб»Ҹ; khГҙng cбә§n server Node.js riГӘng Д‘б»ғ chбәЎy dashboard (chб»ү cбә§n `npm run dev` cho dev, `npm run build` + serve static cho prod-sim).

---

## CORS Configuration (gateway)

VГ¬ dashboard (`:5173`) gб»Қi gateway (`:8080`) khГЎc origin, gateway phбәЈi cбәҘu hГ¬nh CORS:

```yaml
spring:
  cloud:
    gateway:
      globalcors:
        cors-configurations:
          '[/**]':
            allowedOrigins:
              - "http://localhost:5173"
            allowedMethods: ["GET","POST","DELETE","OPTIONS"]
            allowedHeaders: ["*"]
            allowCredentials: false
```

---

## Tech stack chi tiбәҝt

| Layer | ThЖ° viб»Үn | LГҪ do |
|-------|---------|-------|
| UI framework | React 18 | Prereq; hooks ecosystem |
| Build tool | Vite 5 | Dev speed; Vite + React plugin |
| Routing | React Router v6 | Standard; file-based optional |
| Data fetching | TanStack Query v5 | Cache, invalidation, loading state tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng |
| HTTP client | Axios | Interceptors tiб»Үn lб»Јi (gбәҜn X-API-Key tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng) |
| UI components | shadcn/ui hoбә·c Mantine 8 | Component Д‘бә№p, khГҙng custom tб»« Д‘бә§u |
| State (global) | Zustand (nбәҝu cбә§n) | Nhбә№ hЖЎn Redux cho usecase nГ y |

---

## Consequences

**TГӯch cб»ұc:**
- NgЖ°б»қi hб»Қc khГҙng bб»Ӣ distract bб»ҹi FE framework mб»ӣi вҖ” focus vГ o Spring Boot + microservices.
- Build output lГ  static files вҖ” cГі thб»ғ serve bбәұng nginx container trong profile `full`, khГҙng cбә§n Node.js runtime trong production.
- Cб»ҷng Д‘б»“ng React lб»ӣn вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc dб»… tГ¬m tГ i liб»Үu hЖЎn.

**ДҗГЎnh Д‘б»•i / hбәЎn chбәҝ:**
- `dashboard/` khГҙng phбәЈi Gradle subproject вҖ” CI/CD cбә§n 2 pipeline riГӘng (Gradle + npm) hoбә·c dГ№ng Gradle plugin wrapper (khГҙng cбә§n thiбәҝt cho Lab).
- Nбәҝu sau nГ y cбә§n SSR (SEO, initial load performance) вҖ” phбәЈi migrate sang Next.js hoбә·c Remix; khГҙng phбәЈi vбәҘn Д‘б»Ғ vб»ӣi authenticated dashboard.

## CГўy thЖ° mб»Ҙc

```

в””в”Җв”Җ gradle.properties        # JVM args, caching, parallel
```

## Quy Ж°б»ӣc ranh giб»ӣi service (db-per-service)

**NguyГӘn tбәҜc:** mб»—i service sб»ҹ hб»Ҝu database riГӘng вҖ” khГҙng service nГ o Д‘Ж°б»Јc query trб»ұc tiбәҝp DB cб»§a service khГЎc.

| ДҗЖ°б»Јc phГ©p | Bб»Ӣ cбәҘm |
|-----------|--------|
| `implementation(project(":common"))` | `implementation(project(":identity"))` |
| Giao tiбәҝp qua REST nб»ҷi bб»ҷ | Import class domain cб»§a service khГЎc |
| Publish/consume RabbitMQ event | Truy cбәӯp thбәіng DB cб»§a service khГЎc |

`common/` chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc chб»©a **Event DTO** (Java record thuбә§n, khГҙng Spring, khГҙng JPA). Nбәҝu cбә§n thГӘm thб»© gГ¬ khГЎc vГ o common вҶ’ hб»Ҹi lбәЎi thiбәҝt kбәҝ trЖ°б»ӣc.

## Nhб»Ӣp commit-per-step

Mб»—i bЖ°б»ӣc trong Blueprint 10 Chбә·ng tЖ°ЖЎng б»©ng mб»ҷt commit Д‘б»ҷc lбәӯp, Д‘бә·t tГӘn theo pattern:

```
[step-X.Y] mГҙ tбәЈ ngбәҜn
```

VГӯ dб»Ҙ: `[step-1.3] Gradle multi-project skeleton`

Lб»Јi Гӯch: `git checkout <commit-id>` khГҙi phб»Ҙc Д‘Гәng trбәЎng thГЎi cб»§a bЖ°б»ӣc Д‘Гі вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc xem Д‘Ж°б»Јc cбәЈ quГЎ trГ¬nh tiбәҝn hoГЎ, khГҙng chб»ү kбәҝt quбәЈ cuб»‘i.

## CГЎch chбәЎy build (sau khi cГі Gradle wrapper)

```bash
# Build tбәҘt cбәЈ subproject
./gradlew build

# Build riГӘng mб»ҷt service
./gradlew :identity:build

# ChбәЎy tбәҘt cбәЈ test
./gradlew test

# Khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng hбәЎ tбә§ng вҖ” profile core (gateway + identity + identity-db)
cd infra
cp .env.example .env  # Д‘iб»Ғn password thбәӯt vГ o .env
docker compose --profile core up -d

# Khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng toГ n bб»ҷ
docker compose --profile full up -d
```

## Profile Docker Compose

| Profile | Services khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng |
|---------|-------------------|
| `core` | gateway, identity, identity-db |
| `feed` | rabbitmq, market-feed |
| `processing` | rabbitmq, aggregation, aggregation-db, rule-engine, rule-engine-db |
| `delivery` | rabbitmq, alert-delivery, alert-delivery-db, billing, billing-db, mailhog |
| `full` | tбәҘt cбәЈ + dashboard |

CГЎc profile cГі thб»ғ kбәҝt hб»Јp: `--profile core --profile feed` Д‘б»ғ chбәЎy tб»« gateway Д‘бәҝn market-feed.
20:T64d,package com.marketpulse.identity.domain;

import jakarta.persistence.*;
import org.hibernate.annotations.CreationTimestamp;

import java.time.OffsetDateTime;
import java.util.UUID;

@Entity
@Table(name = "api_keys")
public class ApiKey {

    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.UUID)
    private UUID id;

    @ManyToOne(fetch = FetchType.LAZY)
    @JoinColumn(name = "tenant_id", nullable = false)
    private Tenant tenant;

    @Column(name = "key_hash", nullable = false, unique = true, length = 64)
    private String keyHash;

    @Column(length = 100)
    private String label;

    @CreationTimestamp
    @Column(name = "created_at", nullable = false, updatable = false)
    private OffsetDateTime createdAt;

    @Column(name = "revoked_at")
    private OffsetDateTime revokedAt;

    @Column(name = "last_used_at")
    private OffsetDateTime lastUsedAt;

    protected ApiKey() {}

    public ApiKey(Tenant tenant, String keyHash, String label) {
        this.tenant = tenant;
        this.keyHash = keyHash;
        this.label = label;
    }

    public void revoke() {
        this.revokedAt = OffsetDateTime.now();
    }

    public void markUsed() {
        this.lastUsedAt = OffsetDateTime.now();
    }

    public UUID getId() { return id; }
    public Tenant getTenant() { return tenant; }
    public String getKeyHash() { return keyHash; }
    public String getLabel() { return label; }
    public OffsetDateTime getCreatedAt() { return createdAt; }
    public OffsetDateTime getRevokedAt() { return revokedAt; }
    public OffsetDateTime getLastUsedAt() { return lastUsedAt; }
}
21:T4cb,package com.marketpulse.identity.repository;

import com.marketpulse.identity.domain.ApiKey;
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.JpaRepository;
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.Modifying;
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.Query;
import org.springframework.data.repository.query.Param;
import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;

import java.time.OffsetDateTime;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

public interface ApiKeyRepository extends JpaRepository<ApiKey, UUID> {

    List<ApiKey> findByTenant_Id(UUID tenantId);

    Optional<ApiKey> findByIdAndTenant_Id(UUID id, UUID tenantId);

    // Fetch tenant + plan trong cГ№ng 1 query вҖ” dГ№ng cho internal endpoint
    @Query("""
            SELECT k FROM ApiKey k
            JOIN FETCH k.tenant t
            JOIN FETCH t.plan
            WHERE k.keyHash = :keyHash AND k.revokedAt IS NULL
            """)
    Optional<ApiKey> findActiveByKeyHash(@Param("keyHash") String keyHash);

    @Transactional
    @Modifying
    @Query("UPDATE ApiKey k SET k.lastUsedAt = :now WHERE k.id = :id")
    void updateLastUsedAt(@Param("id") UUID id, @Param("now") OffsetDateTime now);
}
22:Tb79,package com.marketpulse.identity.service;

import com.marketpulse.identity.domain.ApiKey;
import com.marketpulse.identity.domain.Tenant;
import com.marketpulse.identity.dto.CreateKeyResponse;
import com.marketpulse.identity.dto.KeySummaryResponse;
import com.marketpulse.identity.exception.KeyNotFoundException;
import com.marketpulse.identity.repository.ApiKeyRepository;
import com.marketpulse.identity.repository.TenantRepository;
import com.marketpulse.identity.util.Sha256;
import org.springframework.scheduling.annotation.Async;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;

import java.security.SecureRandom;
import java.time.OffsetDateTime;
import java.util.HexFormat;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class ApiKeyService {

    private final ApiKeyRepository apiKeyRepository;
    private final TenantRepository tenantRepository;

    public ApiKeyService(ApiKeyRepository apiKeyRepository, TenantRepository tenantRepository) {
        this.apiKeyRepository = apiKeyRepository;
        this.tenantRepository = tenantRepository;
    }

    @Transactional
    public CreateKeyResponse issue(UUID tenantId, String label) {
        Tenant tenant = tenantRepository.findById(tenantId)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException("Tenant not found: " + tenantId));

        // "mp_" + 32 hex chars = 35 kГҪ tб»ұ, Д‘б»§ entropy (128 bit)
        byte[] bytes = new byte[16];
        new SecureRandom().nextBytes(bytes);
        String rawKey = "mp_" + HexFormat.of().formatHex(bytes);
        String keyHash = Sha256.hex(rawKey);

        ApiKey saved = apiKeyRepository.saveAndFlush(new ApiKey(tenant, keyHash, label));
        return new CreateKeyResponse(saved.getId(), rawKey, saved.getLabel(), saved.getCreatedAt());
    }

    @Transactional(readOnly = true)
    public List<KeySummaryResponse> listByTenant(UUID tenantId) {
        return apiKeyRepository.findByTenant_Id(tenantId).stream()
                .map(k -> new KeySummaryResponse(
                        k.getId(), k.getLabel(), k.getCreatedAt(),
                        k.getLastUsedAt(), k.getRevokedAt() != null))
                .toList();
    }

    @Transactional
    public void revoke(UUID tenantId, UUID keyId) {
        ApiKey key = apiKeyRepository.findByIdAndTenant_Id(keyId, tenantId)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new KeyNotFoundException(keyId));
        // Д‘ГЈ revoke вҶ’ coi nhЖ° khГҙng tб»“n tбәЎi
        if (key.getRevokedAt() != null) {
            throw new KeyNotFoundException(keyId);
        }
        key.revoke(); // dirty-checking flush khi transaction commit
    }

    // ChбәЎy async trong thread riГӘng вҖ” khГҙng block response cб»§a internal endpoint
    @Async
    @Transactional
    public void updateLastUsedAtAsync(UUID keyId) {
        apiKeyRepository.updateLastUsedAt(keyId, OffsetDateTime.now());
    }
}
23:T12d5,package com.marketpulse.identity.service;

import com.marketpulse.identity.domain.ApiKey;
import com.marketpulse.identity.domain.Tenant;
import com.marketpulse.identity.dto.CreateKeyResponse;
import com.marketpulse.identity.dto.KeySummaryResponse;
import com.marketpulse.identity.exception.KeyNotFoundException;
import com.marketpulse.identity.repository.ApiKeyRepository;
import com.marketpulse.identity.repository.TenantRepository;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtendWith;
import org.mockito.InjectMocks;
import org.mockito.Mock;
import org.mockito.junit.jupiter.MockitoExtension;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;
import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThatThrownBy;
import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.any;
import static org.mockito.Mockito.*;

@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class)
class ApiKeyServiceTest {

    @Mock
    private ApiKeyRepository apiKeyRepository;

    @Mock
    private TenantRepository tenantRepository;

    @InjectMocks
    private ApiKeyService apiKeyService;

    @Test
    void issue_existingTenant_returnsRawKeyWithPrefix() {
        UUID tenantId = UUID.randomUUID();
        Tenant mockTenant = mock(Tenant.class);

        when(tenantRepository.findById(tenantId)).thenReturn(Optional.of(mockTenant));
        when(apiKeyRepository.saveAndFlush(any(ApiKey.class))).thenAnswer(inv -> inv.getArgument(0));

        CreateKeyResponse response = apiKeyService.issue(tenantId, "production");

        assertThat(response.key()).startsWith("mp_");
        assertThat(response.key()).hasSize(35); // "mp_" + 32 hex chars
        assertThat(response.label()).isEqualTo("production");
        verify(apiKeyRepository).saveAndFlush(any(ApiKey.class));
    }

    @Test
    void issue_twoCallsSameTenant_generateDistinctRawKeys() {
        UUID tenantId = UUID.randomUUID();
        Tenant mockTenant = mock(Tenant.class);

        when(tenantRepository.findById(tenantId)).thenReturn(Optional.of(mockTenant));
        when(apiKeyRepository.saveAndFlush(any(ApiKey.class))).thenAnswer(inv -> inv.getArgument(0));

        String key1 = apiKeyService.issue(tenantId, "a").key();
        String key2 = apiKeyService.issue(tenantId, "b").key();

        assertThat(key1).isNotEqualTo(key2);
    }

    @Test
    void issue_unknownTenant_throwsIllegalState() {
        UUID tenantId = UUID.randomUUID();
        when(tenantRepository.findById(tenantId)).thenReturn(Optional.empty());

        assertThatThrownBy(() -> apiKeyService.issue(tenantId, "x"))
                .isInstanceOf(IllegalStateException.class);
    }

    @Test
    void revoke_activeKey_marksRevoked() {
        UUID tenantId = UUID.randomUUID();
        UUID keyId = UUID.randomUUID();
        Tenant mockTenant = mock(Tenant.class);
        ApiKey key = new ApiKey(mockTenant, "somehash", "label");

        when(apiKeyRepository.findByIdAndTenant_Id(keyId, tenantId))
                .thenReturn(Optional.of(key));

        apiKeyService.revoke(tenantId, keyId);

        assertThat(key.getRevokedAt()).isNotNull();
    }

    @Test
    void revoke_alreadyRevokedKey_throwsKeyNotFound() {
        UUID tenantId = UUID.randomUUID();
        UUID keyId = UUID.randomUUID();
        Tenant mockTenant = mock(Tenant.class);
        ApiKey key = new ApiKey(mockTenant, "somehash", "label");
        key.revoke(); // Д‘ГЈ revoke trЖ°б»ӣc Д‘Гі

        when(apiKeyRepository.findByIdAndTenant_Id(keyId, tenantId))
                .thenReturn(Optional.of(key));

        assertThatThrownBy(() -> apiKeyService.revoke(tenantId, keyId))
                .isInstanceOf(KeyNotFoundException.class);
    }

    @Test
    void revoke_keyNotBelongToTenant_throwsKeyNotFound() {
        UUID tenantId = UUID.randomUUID();
        UUID keyId = UUID.randomUUID();
        when(apiKeyRepository.findByIdAndTenant_Id(keyId, tenantId))
                .thenReturn(Optional.empty());

        assertThatThrownBy(() -> apiKeyService.revoke(tenantId, keyId))
                .isInstanceOf(KeyNotFoundException.class);
    }

    @Test
    void listByTenant_mixedKeys_mapsRevokedFlagCorrectly() {
        UUID tenantId = UUID.randomUUID();
        Tenant mockTenant = mock(Tenant.class);

        ApiKey active = new ApiKey(mockTenant, "hash1", "active-key");
        ApiKey revoked = new ApiKey(mockTenant, "hash2", "revoked-key");
        revoked.revoke();

        when(apiKeyRepository.findByTenant_Id(tenantId)).thenReturn(List.of(active, revoked));

        List<KeySummaryResponse> result = apiKeyService.listByTenant(tenantId);

        assertThat(result).hasSize(2);
        assertThat(result.get(0).revoked()).isFalse();
        assertThat(result.get(1).revoked()).isTrue();
    }
}

import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

@RestController
public class KeyController {

    private final ApiKeyService apiKeyService;

    public KeyController(ApiKeyService apiKeyService) {
        this.apiKeyService = apiKeyService;
    }

    @PostMapping("/api/v1/keys")
    public CreateKeyResponse createKey(
            @RequestHeader("X-Tenant-Id") UUID tenantId,
            @Valid @RequestBody CreateKeyRequest request
    ) {
        return apiKeyService.issue(tenantId, request.label());
    }

    @GetMapping("/api/v1/keys")
    public List<KeySummaryResponse> listKeys(
            @RequestHeader("X-Tenant-Id") UUID tenantId
    ) {
        return apiKeyService.listByTenant(tenantId);
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/api/v1/keys/{id}")
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.NO_CONTENT)
    public void deleteKey(
            @RequestHeader("X-Tenant-Id") UUID tenantId,
            @PathVariable UUID id
    ) {
        apiKeyService.revoke(tenantId, id);
    }
}
25:T4ae,package com.marketpulse.identity.web;

import com.marketpulse.identity.dto.ErrorResponse;
import com.marketpulse.identity.exception.KeyNotFoundException;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
import org.springframework.web.bind.MethodArgumentNotValidException;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.ExceptionHandler;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.ResponseStatus;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestControllerAdvice;

@RestControllerAdvice
public class GlobalExceptionHandler {

    @ExceptionHandler(KeyNotFoundException.class)
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND)
    public ErrorResponse handleKeyNotFound(KeyNotFoundException e) {
        return new ErrorResponse("KEY_NOT_FOUND");
    }

    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST)
    public ErrorResponse handleValidation(MethodArgumentNotValidException e) {
        String message = e.getBindingResult().getFieldErrors().stream()
                .map(fe -> fe.getField() + " " + fe.getDefaultMessage())
                .findFirst()
                .orElse("INVALID_REQUEST");
        return new ErrorResponse(message);
    }
}

        this.apiKeyRepository = apiKeyRepository;
        this.apiKeyService = apiKeyService;
    }

    // Chб»ү dГ№ng nб»ҷi bб»ҷ Docker network вҖ” gateway gб»Қi Д‘б»ғ xГЎc thб»ұc raw key
    @GetMapping("/internal/keys/{keyHash}")
    public InternalKeyResponse getByHash(@PathVariable String keyHash) {
        ApiKey key = apiKeyRepository.findActiveByKeyHash(keyHash)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new KeyNotFoundException(keyHash));

        // Cбәӯp nhбәӯt last_used_at khГҙng chбә·n response
        apiKeyService.updateLastUsedAtAsync(key.getId());

        return new InternalKeyResponse(
                key.getTenant().getId(),
                key.getTenant().getPlan().getId(),
                "ACTIVE"
        );
    }
}

28:T1519,package com.marketpulse.gateway.filter;

import com.github.benmanes.caffeine.cache.Cache;
import com.github.benmanes.caffeine.cache.Caffeine;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.cloud.gateway.filter.GatewayFilterChain;
import org.springframework.cloud.gateway.filter.GlobalFilter;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
import org.springframework.http.MediaType;
import org.springframework.http.server.reactive.ServerHttpRequest;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.function.client.WebClient;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.function.client.WebClientResponseException;
import org.springframework.web.server.ServerWebExchange;
import reactor.core.publisher.Mono;

import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.security.MessageDigest;
import java.security.NoSuchAlgorithmException;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

/**
 * Auth filter chбәЎy trЖ°б»ӣc mб»Қi route filter.
 * Flow: X-API-Key вҶ’ SHA-256 вҶ’ Caffeine cache(TTL 5s) вҶ’ identity lookup вҶ’ forward vб»ӣi X-Tenant-Id.
 * LoбәЎi trб»« /actuator/** Д‘б»ғ compose healthcheck hoбәЎt Д‘б»ҷng.
 */
@Component
public class ApiKeyAuthFilter implements GlobalFilter, Ordered {

    private static final String HEADER_API_KEY = "X-API-Key";
    private static final String HEADER_TENANT_ID = "X-Tenant-Id";

    private final WebClient webClient;
    // Optional.of(tenantId) = active key; Optional.empty() = revoked/not-found (negative cache)
    private final Cache<String, Optional<String>> keyCache;

    public ApiKeyAuthFilter(@Value("${identity.service.url}") String identityServiceUrl) {
        this.webClient = WebClient.builder().baseUrl(identityServiceUrl).build();
        this.keyCache = Caffeine.newBuilder()
                .expireAfterWrite(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
                .maximumSize(10_000)
                .build();
    }

    @Override
    public int getOrder() {
        return Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE;
    }

    @Override
    public Mono<Void> filter(ServerWebExchange exchange, GatewayFilterChain chain) {
        String path = exchange.getRequest().getURI().getPath();
        if (path.startsWith("/actuator")) {
            return chain.filter(exchange);
        }

        String rawKey = exchange.getRequest().getHeaders().getFirst(HEADER_API_KEY);
        if (rawKey == null || rawKey.isBlank()) {
            return reject(exchange, HttpStatus.UNAUTHORIZED, "MISSING_API_KEY");
        }

        String keyHash = sha256Hex(rawKey);

        Optional<String> cached = keyCache.getIfPresent(keyHash);
        if (cached != null) {
            if (cached.isEmpty()) {
                return reject(exchange, HttpStatus.UNAUTHORIZED, "INVALID_API_KEY");
            }
            return forward(exchange, chain, cached.get());
        }

        return webClient.get()
                .uri("/internal/keys/" + keyHash)
                .retrieve()
                .bodyToMono(KeyLookupResponse.class)
                .timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(2))
                .flatMap(resp -> {
                    keyCache.put(keyHash, Optional.of(resp.tenantId()));
                    return forward(exchange, chain, resp.tenantId());
                })
                .onErrorResume(e -> {
                    if (e instanceof WebClientResponseException wex && wex.getStatusCode().value() == 404) {
                        keyCache.put(keyHash, Optional.empty());
                        return reject(exchange, HttpStatus.UNAUTHORIZED, "INVALID_API_KEY");
                    }
                    // 5xx hoбә·c timeout вҖ” khГҙng cache Д‘б»ғ gateway thб»ӯ lбәЎi khi identity hб»“i phб»Ҙc
                    return reject(exchange, HttpStatus.SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE, "IDENTITY_UNAVAILABLE");
                });
    }

    private Mono<Void> forward(ServerWebExchange exchange, GatewayFilterChain chain, String tenantId) {
        ServerHttpRequest mutated = exchange.getRequest().mutate()
                .header(HEADER_TENANT_ID, tenantId)
                .headers(h -> h.remove(HEADER_API_KEY))
                .build();
        return chain.filter(exchange.mutate().request(mutated).build());
    }

    private Mono<Void> reject(ServerWebExchange exchange, HttpStatus status, String errorCode) {
        exchange.getResponse().setStatusCode(status);
        exchange.getResponse().getHeaders().setContentType(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON);
        byte[] body = ("{\"error\":\"" + errorCode + "\"}").getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
        return exchange.getResponse().writeWith(
                Mono.just(exchange.getResponse().bufferFactory().wrap(body)));
    }

    private static String sha256Hex(String input) {
        try {
            MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
            byte[] hash = md.digest(input.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(64);
            for (byte b : hash) {
                sb.append(String.format("%02x", b));
            }
            return sb.toString();
        } catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException e) {
            throw new IllegalStateException("SHA-256 unavailable", e);
        }
    }

    private record KeyLookupResponse(String tenantId, String planId, String status) {}
}

2b:T444,package com.marketpulse.marketfeed.publisher;

import com.marketpulse.common.event.TradeEvent;
import com.marketpulse.marketfeed.config.RabbitConfig;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.amqp.rabbit.core.RabbitTemplate;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
public class TradePublisher {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TradePublisher.class);

    private final RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;

    public TradePublisher(RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate) {
        this.rabbitTemplate = rabbitTemplate;
    }

    public void publish(TradeEvent event) {
        publish(event, false);
    }

    public void publish(TradeEvent event, boolean replay) {
        rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend(RabbitConfig.EXCHANGE_NAME, event.symbol(), event, msg -> {
            if (replay) {
                msg.getMessageProperties().setHeader("x-replay", true);
            }
            return msg;
        });
        log.debug("Published trade: symbol={} price={}", event.symbol(), event.price());
    }
}
2c:T656,package com.marketpulse.marketfeed.binance;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.marketpulse.common.event.TradeEvent;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.Optional;

@Component
public class BinanceTradeMapper {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BinanceTradeMapper.class);

    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;

    public BinanceTradeMapper(ObjectMapper objectMapper) {
        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
    }

    /**
     * Parses a Binance combined-stream message.
     * Format: {"stream":"btcusdt@trade","data":{"e":"trade","s":"BTCUSDT","p":"...","q":"...","t":123,"T":456,...}}
     * Returns empty if not a trade event or if parsing fails.
     */
    public Optional<TradeEvent> map(String json) {
        try {
            JsonNode root = objectMapper.readTree(json);
            JsonNode data = root.path("data");
            if (data.isMissingNode() || !"trade".equals(data.path("e").asText())) {
                return Optional.empty();
            }
            return Optional.of(new TradeEvent(
                    data.path("s").asText(),
                    data.path("p").asText(),
                    data.path("q").asText(),
                    data.path("t").asLong(),
                    data.path("T").asLong()
            ));
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.warn("Failed to parse Binance message: {}", e.getMessage());
            return Optional.empty();
        }
    }
}
2d:T512,class BinanceTradeMapperTest {

    private final BinanceTradeMapper mapper = new BinanceTradeMapper(new ObjectMapper());

    @Test
    void parsesValidTradeMessage() {
        String json = """
                {"stream":"btcusdt@trade","data":{"e":"trade","E":1234567890123,"s":"BTCUSDT","t":123456,"p":"49850.00","q":"0.001","T":1234567890000,"m":true}}
                """.trim();

        Optional<TradeEvent> result = mapper.map(json);

        assertThat(result).isPresent();
        TradeEvent event = result.get();
        assertThat(event.symbol()).isEqualTo("BTCUSDT");
        assertThat(event.price()).isEqualTo("49850.00");
        assertThat(event.quantity()).isEqualTo("0.001");
        assertThat(event.tradeId()).isEqualTo(123456L);
        assertThat(event.tradeTime()).isEqualTo(1234567890000L);
    }

    @Test
    void returnsEmptyForGarbageMessage() {
        Optional<TradeEvent> result = mapper.map("not-valid-json{{{");
        assertThat(result).isEmpty();
    }

    @Test
    void returnsEmptyForNonTradeMessage() {
        String json = """
                {"stream":"btcusdt@depthUpdate","data":{"e":"depthUpdate","E":1234567890123}}
                """.trim();

        Optional<TradeEvent> result = mapper.map(json);

        assertThat(result).isEmpty();
    }
}
2e:Tfa8,@Component
@ConditionalOnProperty(name = "feed.mode", havingValue = "live", matchIfMissing = true)
public class LiveFeed implements ApplicationRunner {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(LiveFeed.class);

    private final FeedProperties feedProperties;
    private final BinanceTradeMapper mapper;
    private final TradePublisher publisher;

    private final OkHttpClient httpClient = new OkHttpClient.Builder()
            .pingInterval(20, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
            .build();
    private final ScheduledExecutorService scheduler = Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(r -> {
        Thread t = new Thread(r, "livefeed-reconnect");
        t.setDaemon(true);
        return t;
    });
    private final AtomicInteger reconnectAttempts = new AtomicInteger(0);
    private final AtomicBoolean firstTradeLogged = new AtomicBoolean(false);
    private volatile boolean running = false;
    private volatile WebSocket webSocket;

    public LiveFeed(FeedProperties feedProperties, BinanceTradeMapper mapper, TradePublisher publisher) {
        this.feedProperties = feedProperties;
        this.mapper = mapper;
        this.publisher = publisher;
    }

    @Override
    public void run(ApplicationArguments args) {
        start();
    }

    public void start() {
        running = true;
        String url = buildWsUrl();
        Request request = new Request.Builder().url(url).build();
        webSocket = httpClient.newWebSocket(request, new TradeWebSocketListener());
    }

    @PreDestroy
    public void stop() {
        running = false;
        if (webSocket != null) {
            webSocket.close(1000, "Service shutting down");
        }
        scheduler.shutdown();
        httpClient.dispatcher().executorService().shutdown();
    }

    // Combined-stream URL: wss://.../stream?streams=btcusdt@trade/ethusdt@trade
    private String buildWsUrl() {
        String streams = feedProperties.symbols().stream()
                .map(s -> s.toLowerCase() + "@trade")
                .collect(Collectors.joining("/"));
        return feedProperties.binanceWsUrl() + "?streams=" + streams;
    }

    private void scheduleReconnect() {
        if (!running || scheduler.isShutdown()) {
            return;
        }
        int attempt = reconnectAttempts.incrementAndGet();
        if (attempt > feedProperties.reconnectMaxAttempts()) {
            log.error("Max reconnect attempts ({}) reached, giving up", feedProperties.reconnectMaxAttempts());
            return;
        }
        log.warn("Scheduling reconnect attempt {}/{} in {}s",
                attempt, feedProperties.reconnectMaxAttempts(), feedProperties.reconnectDelaySeconds());
        scheduler.schedule(this::start, feedProperties.reconnectDelaySeconds(), TimeUnit.SECONDS);
    }

    private class TradeWebSocketListener extends WebSocketListener {

        @Override
        public void onOpen(WebSocket webSocket, Response response) {
            reconnectAttempts.set(0);
            firstTradeLogged.set(false);
            log.info("Connected to Binance WS: {}", buildWsUrl());
        }

        @Override
        public void onMessage(WebSocket webSocket, String text) {
            mapper.map(text).ifPresent(event -> {
                if (firstTradeLogged.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
                    log.info("First trade received: symbol={} price={}", event.symbol(), event.price());
                }
                publisher.publish(event);
            });
        }

        @Override
        public void onFailure(WebSocket webSocket, Throwable t, Response response) {
            log.warn("Binance WS failure: {}", t.getMessage());
            scheduleReconnect();
        }

        @Override
        public void onClosed(WebSocket webSocket, int code, String reason) {
            if (code != 1000) {
                log.warn("Binance WS closed unexpectedly: code={} reason={}", code, reason);
                scheduleReconnect();
            }
        }
    }
}
2f:T4df,/**
 * Reusable Binance combined-stream WebSocket client with auto-reconnect.
 * Call start(callback) to open the connection; stop() to close it cleanly.
 * Shared by LiveFeed (publish only) and RecordFeed (publish + write NDJSON).
 */
@Component
public class BinanceWsClient {

    private final FeedProperties feedProperties;
    private final BinanceTradeMapper mapper;
    // ... OkHttpClient, scheduler, reconnect state вҖ” y hб»Үt LiveFeed cЕ© ...

    public void start(Consumer<TradeEvent> onTrade) {
        this.tradeConsumer = onTrade;
        running = true;
        connect();
    }

    public void stop() { /* Д‘Гіng WS, tбәҜt scheduler */ }

    private class Listener extends WebSocketListener {
        @Override
        public void onMessage(WebSocket webSocket, String text) {
            mapper.map(text).ifPresent(event -> {
                if (firstTradeLogged.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
                    log.info("First trade received: symbol={} price={}", event.symbol(), event.price());
                }
                tradeConsumer.accept(event);   // khГЎc LiveFeed cЕ©: gб»Қi callback, khГҙng publish thбәіng
            });
        }
        // onOpen/onFailure/onClosed giб»Ҝ nguyГӘn logic reconnect
    }
}
30:T619,@Component
@ConditionalOnProperty(name = "feed.mode", havingValue = "record")
public class RecordFeed {

    // key = "SYMBOL-yyyy-MM-dd" вҖ” rotates writers automatically at date boundary
    private final Map<String, BufferedWriter> writers = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

    public void start() {
        wsClient.start(this::onTrade);
    }

    private void onTrade(TradeEvent event) {
        publisher.publish(event);
        writeNdJson(event);
    }

    private void writeNdJson(TradeEvent event) {
        LocalDate date = LocalDate.now(ZoneOffset.UTC);
        String key = event.symbol() + "-" + date;
        try {
            BufferedWriter writer = writers.computeIfAbsent(key, k -> openWriter(event.symbol(), date));
            writer.write(objectMapper.writeValueAsString(event));
            writer.newLine();
            writer.flush();
        } catch (IOException | UncheckedIOException e) {
            log.error("Failed to write NDJSON for symbol={} date={}: {}", event.symbol(), date, e.getMessage());
        }
    }

    private BufferedWriter openWriter(String symbol, LocalDate date) {
        Path dir = Path.of(feedProperties.dataPath());
        Files.createDirectories(dir);
        Path file = dir.resolve("trades-" + symbol + "-" + date + ".ndjson");
        return Files.newBufferedWriter(file, StandardOpenOption.CREATE, StandardOpenOption.APPEND);
    }

    @PreDestroy
    public void stop() {
        wsClient.stop();
        writers.values().forEach(w -> { try { w.close(); } catch (IOException ignored) {} });
    }
}
31:T913,@Component
@ConditionalOnProperty(name = "feed.mode", havingValue = "replay")
public class ReplayFeed {

    // gaps larger than this (e.g. missing data in file) are clamped to 0 so replay does not stall
    static final long MAX_DELTA_MS = 60_000L;

    public void start() {
        running = true;
        replayThread = Thread.ofVirtual().name("replay-feed").start(this::replayLoop);
    }

    private void replayLoop() {
        Path file = Path.of(replayProperties.file());
        int totalReplayed = 0;
        boolean firstIteration = true;
        do {
            if (!firstIteration) {
                log.info("Replay loop: restarting from beginning of {}", file.getFileName());
            }
            firstIteration = false;
            totalReplayed += replayFile(file);
        } while (running && replayProperties.loop());
    }

    private int replayFile(Path file) throws IOException {
        int count = 0;
        long prevTradeTime = -1;
        try (BufferedReader reader = Files.newBufferedReader(file)) {
            String line;
            while (running && (line = reader.readLine()) != null) {
                if (line.isBlank()) continue;
                TradeEvent event = objectMapper.readValue(line, TradeEvent.class);
                long sleepMs = computeSleepMs(prevTradeTime, event.tradeTime(), replayProperties.multiplier());
                if (sleepMs > 0) Thread.sleep(sleepMs);
                publisher.publish(event, true);   // true = gбәҜn header x-replay
                prevTradeTime = event.tradeTime();
                count++;
            }
        }
        return count;
    }

    /**
     * Time to sleep before emitting the current trade, scaled by multiplier.
     * Returns 0 for the first trade (prevTradeTime == -1), for negative deltas,
     * or when the gap exceeds MAX_DELTA_MS (data gap in the file вҖ” don't stall).
     */
    static long computeSleepMs(long prevTradeTime, long currTradeTime, double multiplier) {
        if (prevTradeTime < 0) return 0;
        long delta = currTradeTime - prevTradeTime;
        if (delta < 0 || delta > MAX_DELTA_MS) return 0;
        return (long) (delta / multiplier);
    }

    @PreDestroy
    public void stop() {
        running = false;
        if (replayThread != null) replayThread.interrupt();
    }
}
32:T478,@Component
public class FeedRunner implements ApplicationRunner {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FeedRunner.class);

    private final Optional<LiveFeed> liveFeed;
    private final Optional<RecordFeed> recordFeed;
    private final Optional<ReplayFeed> replayFeed;

    public FeedRunner(Optional<LiveFeed> liveFeed, Optional<RecordFeed> recordFeed,
                      Optional<ReplayFeed> replayFeed) {
        this.liveFeed = liveFeed;
        this.recordFeed = recordFeed;
        this.replayFeed = replayFeed;
    }

    @Override
    public void run(ApplicationArguments args) {
        if (liveFeed.isPresent()) {
            log.info("Starting feed in LIVE mode");
            liveFeed.get().start();
        } else if (recordFeed.isPresent()) {
            log.info("Starting feed in RECORD mode");
            recordFeed.get().start();
        } else if (replayFeed.isPresent()) {
            log.info("Starting feed in REPLAY mode");
            replayFeed.get().start();
        } else {
            log.warn("No feed started вҖ” check feed.mode property (live/record/replay)");
        }
    }
}
33:T445,class ReplayFeedDeltaTest {

    @Test
    void firstTradeReturnsZeroSleep() {
        assertThat(ReplayFeed.computeSleepMs(-1, 1_000L, 1.0)).isEqualTo(0);
    }

    @Test
    void normalDeltaScaledByMultiplier() {
        // 1000ms gap replayed at 2x speed вҶ’ sleep 500ms
        assertThat(ReplayFeed.computeSleepMs(1_000L, 2_000L, 2.0)).isEqualTo(500L);
    }

    @Test
    void negativeDeltaClampsToZero() {
        assertThat(ReplayFeed.computeSleepMs(2_000L, 1_000L, 1.0)).isEqualTo(0);
    }

    @Test
    void deltaExceedingMaxClampsToZero() {
        long gap = ReplayFeed.MAX_DELTA_MS + 1;
        assertThat(ReplayFeed.computeSleepMs(1_000L, 1_000L + gap, 1.0)).isEqualTo(0);
    }

    @Test
    void exactMaxDeltaIsNotClamped() {
        assertThat(ReplayFeed.computeSleepMs(1_000L, 1_000L + ReplayFeed.MAX_DELTA_MS, 1.0))
                .isEqualTo(ReplayFeed.MAX_DELTA_MS);
    }

    @Test
    void multiplierAboveOneCompressesTime() {
        // 10s gap at 10x speed вҶ’ sleep 1s
        assertThat(ReplayFeed.computeSleepMs(0L, 10_000L, 10.0)).isEqualTo(1_000L);
    }
}
