public class Candle {

    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY)
    private Long id;

    @Column(nullable = false, length = 20)
    private String symbol;

    @Column(name = "open_time", nullable = false)
    private OffsetDateTime openTime;

    @Column(name = "open_price", nullable = false, precision = 20, scale = 8)
    private BigDecimal openPrice;
    @Column(name = "high_price", nullable = false, precision = 20, scale = 8)
    private BigDecimal highPrice;
    @Column(name = "low_price", nullable = false, precision = 20, scale = 8)
    private BigDecimal lowPrice;
    @Column(name = "close_price", nullable = false, precision = 20, scale = 8)
    private BigDecimal closePrice;
    @Column(nullable = false, precision = 20, scale = 8)
    private BigDecimal volume;
    @Column(name = "trade_count", nullable = false)
    private int tradeCount;

    protected Candle() {}

    public static Candle of(String symbol, OffsetDateTime openTime,
                             BigDecimal openPrice, BigDecimal highPrice,
                             BigDecimal lowPrice, BigDecimal closePrice,
                             BigDecimal volume, int tradeCount) {
        Candle c = new Candle();
        c.symbol = symbol;
        c.openTime = openTime;
        c.openPrice = openPrice;
        c.highPrice = highPrice;
        c.lowPrice = lowPrice;
        c.closePrice = closePrice;
        c.volume = volume;
        c.tradeCount = tradeCount;
        return c;
    }

    // getter cho mб»Қi trЖ°б»қng вҖ” khГҙng cГі setter
    public Long getId() { return id; }
    public String getSymbol() { return symbol; }
    public OffsetDateTime getOpenTime() { return openTime; }
    public BigDecimal getOpenPrice() { return openPrice; }
    public BigDecimal getHighPrice() { return highPrice; }
    public BigDecimal getLowPrice() { return lowPrice; }
    public BigDecimal getClosePrice() { return closePrice; }
    public BigDecimal getVolume() { return volume; }
    public int getTradeCount() { return tradeCount; }
}
35:T5b5,@Component
public class CandleAggregator {

    private final ConcurrentHashMap<WindowKey, CandleWindow> windows = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

    public void addTrade(TradeEvent trade) {
        // floor tradeTime to the start of its minute
        long openTimeMs = (trade.tradeTime() / 60_000L) * 60_000L;
        BigDecimal price = new BigDecimal(trade.price());
        BigDecimal qty = new BigDecimal(trade.quantity());
        WindowKey key = new WindowKey(trade.symbol(), openTimeMs);

        // compute holds a per-key lock, serialising concurrent addTrade for the same window
        windows.compute(key, (k, w) -> {
            if (w == null) return new CandleWindow(k.symbol(), k.openTimeMs(), price, qty);
            w.accumulate(price, qty);
            return w;
        });
    }

    /**
     * Returns and removes all windows whose minute has fully elapsed.
     * A window is closed when openTimeMs + 60_000 <= nowEpochMs.
     * The current minute's window is kept in place.
     */
    public List<CandleWindow> drainClosedWindows(long nowEpochMs) {
        List<CandleWindow> closed = new ArrayList<>();
        windows.entrySet().removeIf(entry -> {
            if (entry.getKey().openTimeMs() + 60_000L <= nowEpochMs) {
                closed.add(entry.getValue());
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        });
        return closed;
    }

    record WindowKey(String symbol, long openTimeMs) {}
}
36:T533,public class CandleWindow {

    private final String symbol;
    private final long openTimeMs;
    private BigDecimal open, high, low, close, volume;
    private int tradeCount;

    CandleWindow(String symbol, long openTimeMs, BigDecimal firstPrice, BigDecimal firstQty) {
        this.symbol = symbol;
        this.openTimeMs = openTimeMs;
        this.open = this.high = this.low = this.close = firstPrice;
        this.volume = firstQty;
        this.tradeCount = 1;
    }

    // Called only under ConcurrentHashMap.compute per-key lock вҖ” no extra sync needed.
    void accumulate(BigDecimal price, BigDecimal qty) {
        if (price.compareTo(high) > 0) high = price;
        if (price.compareTo(low) < 0) low = price;
        close = price;
        volume = volume.add(qty);
        tradeCount++;
    }

    public Candle1mEvent toCandle1mEvent() {
        return new Candle1mEvent(symbol, openTimeMs,
                open.toPlainString(), high.toPlainString(),
                low.toPlainString(), close.toPlainString(),
                volume.toPlainString(), tradeCount);
    }

    public Candle toEntity() {
        OffsetDateTime openTime = OffsetDateTime.ofInstant(Instant.ofEpochMilli(openTimeMs), ZoneOffset.UTC);
        return Candle.of(symbol, openTime, open, high, low, close, volume, tradeCount);
    }
}
37:T722,@Component
public class CandleFlusher {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CandleFlusher.class);

    private final CandleAggregator candleAggregator;
    private final CandleRepository candleRepository;
    private final RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;

    public CandleFlusher(CandleAggregator candleAggregator,
                         CandleRepository candleRepository,
                         RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate) {
        this.candleAggregator = candleAggregator;
        this.candleRepository = candleRepository;
        this.rabbitTemplate = rabbitTemplate;
    }

    @Scheduled(fixedDelayString = "${aggregation.flush.flush-interval-ms}")
    public void flush() {
        List<CandleWindow> closed = candleAggregator.drainClosedWindows(System.currentTimeMillis());
        if (closed.isEmpty()) return;

        int flushed = 0;
        for (CandleWindow window : closed) {
            try {
                Candle entity = window.toEntity();
                if (candleRepository.existsBySymbolAndOpenTime(entity.getSymbol(), entity.getOpenTime())) {
                    log.warn("Duplicate candle skipped: {} @ {}", entity.getSymbol(), entity.getOpenTime());
                    continue;
                }
                candleRepository.save(entity);
                rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend(
                        RabbitConfig.CANDLES_EXCHANGE,
                        window.getSymbol() + ".1m",
                        window.toCandle1mEvent());
                flushed++;
            } catch (Exception e) {
                log.error("Failed to flush candle {} @ {}: {}",
                        window.getSymbol(), window.getOpenTimeMs(), e.getMessage(), e);
            }
        }
        if (flushed > 0) log.info("Flushed {} candle(s)", flushed);
    }
}

39:T9ac,@Configuration
public class RabbitConfig {

    public static final String TRADES_EXCHANGE  = "market-pulse.trades";
    public static final String CANDLES_EXCHANGE = "market-pulse.candles";
    public static final String QUOTA_EXCHANGE   = "market-pulse.quota";
    public static final String ALERTS_EXCHANGE  = "market-pulse.alerts";

    public static final String TRADES_QUEUE  = "rule-engine.trades";
    public static final String CANDLES_QUEUE = "rule-engine.candles";
    public static final String QUOTA_QUEUE   = "rule-engine.quota";

    public static final String CANDLES_BINDING_KEY = "*.1m";
    public static final String QUOTA_BINDING_KEY    = "quota.exceeded";
    public static final String ALERTS_ROUTING_KEY    = "alert";

    @Bean public FanoutExchange tradesExchange() { return new FanoutExchange(TRADES_EXCHANGE, true, false); }
    @Bean public TopicExchange candlesExchange() { return new TopicExchange(CANDLES_EXCHANGE, true, false); }
    @Bean public DirectExchange quotaExchange() { return new DirectExchange(QUOTA_EXCHANGE, true, false); }
    // Declare exchange alerts Д‘б»ғ publish; queue do alert-delivery/billing tб»ұ khai (Chбә·ng 6/7).
    @Bean public DirectExchange alertsExchange() { return new DirectExchange(ALERTS_EXCHANGE, true, false); }

    @Bean public Queue tradesQueue() { return new Queue(TRADES_QUEUE, true); }
    @Bean public Queue candlesQueue() { return new Queue(CANDLES_QUEUE, true); }
    @Bean public Queue quotaQueue() { return new Queue(QUOTA_QUEUE, true); }

    @Bean
    public Binding tradesBinding(Queue tradesQueue, FanoutExchange tradesExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(tradesQueue).to(tradesExchange);
    }
    @Bean
    public Binding candlesBinding(Queue candlesQueue, TopicExchange candlesExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(candlesQueue).to(candlesExchange).with(CANDLES_BINDING_KEY);
    }
    @Bean
    public Binding quotaBinding(Queue quotaQueue, DirectExchange quotaExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(quotaQueue).to(quotaExchange).with(QUOTA_BINDING_KEY);
    }

    @Bean
    public Jackson2JsonMessageConverter jackson2JsonMessageConverter() {
        DefaultJackson2JavaTypeMapper typeMapper = new DefaultJackson2JavaTypeMapper();
        typeMapper.setTrustedPackages("com.marketpulse.*");
        Jackson2JsonMessageConverter converter = new Jackson2JsonMessageConverter();
        converter.setClassMapper(typeMapper);
        return converter;
    }
}
3a:T80b,@Service
@Transactional
public class RuleService {

    private static final Set<String> VALID_TYPES = Set.of(
            "PRICE_THRESHOLD", "PERCENT_CHANGE", "VOLUME_SPIKE");

    private static final Map<String, Set<String>> REQUIRED_PARAMS = Map.of(
            "PRICE_THRESHOLD", Set.of("threshold", "direction"),
            "PERCENT_CHANGE",  Set.of("percent", "windowMinutes", "direction"),
            "VOLUME_SPIKE",    Set.of("multiplier")
    );

    // ... constructor(ruleRepository, quotaClient) ...

    public RuleResponse create(UUID tenantId, CreateRuleRequest req) {
        validateSymbol(req.symbol());
        validateTypeAndParams(req.type(), req.params());
        checkQuota(tenantId);

        Rule rule = new Rule(tenantId, req.symbol(), req.type(), req.params(), req.webhookUrl());
        Rule saved = ruleRepository.save(rule);
        // TODO: refresh RuleStore вҖ” bЖ°б»ӣc 5.4
        return toResponse(saved);
    }

    private void validateTypeAndParams(String type, Map<String, Object> params) {
        if (!VALID_TYPES.contains(type)) throw new InvalidParamsException();
        Set<String> required = REQUIRED_PARAMS.get(type);
        if (params == null || !params.keySet().containsAll(required)) {
            throw new InvalidParamsException();
        }
    }

    private void checkQuota(UUID tenantId) {
        try {
            Optional<QuotaStatus> quota = quotaClient.check(tenantId);
            if (quota.isPresent() && quota.get().rulesQuotaExceeded()) {
                long current = ruleRepository.countByTenantIdAndStatus(tenantId, "ACTIVE");
                throw new QuotaExceededException(quota.get().maxRules(), (int) current);
            }
        } catch (QuotaExceededException e) {
            throw e;   // Д‘Гўy lГ  lб»—i NGHIб»ҶP Vб»Ө thбәӯt вҖ” phбәЈi nГ©m tiбәҝp
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.warn("billing unavailable, skipping quota check: {}", e.getMessage());
            // nuб»‘t lб»—i Hбә  TбәҰNG cГі chб»§ Д‘Гӯch вҖ” Д‘Гўy chГӯnh lГ  fail-open
        }
    }
}
3b:T657,@Component
public class RuleStore {

    private final RuleRepository ruleRepository;

    // symbol вҶ’ (ruleId вҶ’ Rule)
    private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, ConcurrentHashMap<UUID, Rule>> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

    @PostConstruct
    public void loadAll() {
        ruleRepository.findByStatus("ACTIVE").forEach(this::upsert);
        log.info("RuleStore loaded {} symbols", store.size());
    }

    /** ThГӘm/cбәӯp nhбәӯt rule; nбәҝu khГҙng phбәЈi ACTIVE thГ¬ remove khб»Ҹi store. */
    public void upsert(Rule rule) {
        if ("ACTIVE".equals(rule.getStatus())) {
            store.computeIfAbsent(rule.getSymbol(), k -> new ConcurrentHashMap<>())
                 .put(rule.getId(), rule);
        } else {
            remove(rule.getId());
        }
    }

    public void remove(UUID ruleId) {
        store.values().forEach(symbolMap -> symbolMap.remove(ruleId));
    }

    /** XГіa khб»Ҹi store mб»Қi rule cб»§a tenant (dГ№ng khi quota vЖ°б»Јt mб»©c вҖ” bЖ°б»ӣc 5.7). */
    public void pauseByTenant(UUID tenantId) {
        store.values().forEach(symbolMap ->
            symbolMap.values().removeIf(r -> tenantId.equals(r.getTenantId())));
    }

    /** BбәЈn sao вҖ” trГЎnh ConcurrentModificationException khi caller Д‘ang lбә·p qua. */
    public List<Rule> forSymbol(String symbol, String ruleType) {
        Map<UUID, Rule> symbolMap = store.get(symbol);
        if (symbolMap == null) return List.of();
        return symbolMap.values().stream()
                .filter(r -> ruleType.equals(r.getRuleType()) && "ACTIVE".equals(r.getStatus()))
                .toList();
    }
}
3c:T6d1,@Component
public class PercentChangeEvaluator {

    /**
     * params: percent (tб»‘i thiб»ғu, luГҙn dЖ°ЖЎng), windowMinutes (sб»‘ nбәҝn nhГ¬n lГ№i),
     *         direction: "UP" (pct вүҘ percent) | "DOWN" (pct вүӨ -percent)
     * recentCandles phбәЈi sбәҜp cЕ© вҶ’ mб»ӣi. Cбә§n Гӯt nhбәҘt windowMinutes + 1 nбәҝn.
     */
    public Optional<AlertTrigger> evaluate(Rule rule, List<Candle1mEvent> recentCandles) {
        BigDecimal percent = new BigDecimal(rule.getParams().get("percent").toString());
        int windowMinutes = Integer.parseInt(rule.getParams().get("windowMinutes").toString());
        String direction = rule.getParams().get("direction").toString();

        if (recentCandles.size() < windowMinutes + 1) {
            return Optional.empty();   // chЖ°a Д‘б»§ lб»Ӣch sб»ӯ Д‘б»ғ so sГЎnh
        }

        Candle1mEvent newest = recentCandles.get(recentCandles.size() - 1);
        Candle1mEvent past   = recentCandles.get(recentCandles.size() - 1 - windowMinutes);

        BigDecimal closeNow  = new BigDecimal(newest.close());
        BigDecimal closePast = new BigDecimal(past.close());
        if (closePast.compareTo(BigDecimal.ZERO) == 0) return Optional.empty();

        BigDecimal pct = closeNow.subtract(closePast)
                .divide(closePast, 8, RoundingMode.HALF_UP)
                .multiply(BigDecimal.valueOf(100))
                .setScale(4, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);

        boolean triggered = switch (direction) {
            case "UP"   -> pct.compareTo(percent) >= 0;
            case "DOWN" -> pct.compareTo(percent.negate()) <= 0;
            default     -> false;
        };
        return triggered ? Optional.of(new AlertTrigger(rule, pct.toPlainString())) : Optional.empty();
    }
}
3d:T56a,@Component
public class VolumeSpikeEvaluator {

    /**
     * params.multiplier вҖ“ hб»Ү sб»‘ nhГўn so vб»ӣi baseline.
     * baseline = trung bГ¬nh volume cб»§a Mб»ҢI nбәҝn ngoбәЎi trб»« nбәҝn mб»ӣi nhбәҘt (tб»‘i Д‘a 59 nбәҝn).
     * Trigger khi volume nбәҝn mб»ӣi nhбәҘt вүҘ multiplier Г— baseline.
     */
    public Optional<AlertTrigger> evaluate(Rule rule, List<Candle1mEvent> recentCandles) {
        if (recentCandles.size() < 2) return Optional.empty();

        BigDecimal multiplier = new BigDecimal(rule.getParams().get("multiplier").toString());
        Candle1mEvent current = recentCandles.get(recentCandles.size() - 1);
        List<Candle1mEvent> baseline = recentCandles.subList(0, recentCandles.size() - 1);

        BigDecimal totalVolume = baseline.stream()
                .map(c -> new BigDecimal(c.volume()))
                .reduce(BigDecimal.ZERO, BigDecimal::add);
        BigDecimal avgVolume = totalVolume.divide(
                BigDecimal.valueOf(baseline.size()), 8, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
        if (avgVolume.compareTo(BigDecimal.ZERO) == 0) return Optional.empty();

        BigDecimal currentVolume = new BigDecimal(current.volume());
        boolean triggered = currentVolume.compareTo(multiplier.multiply(avgVolume)) >= 0;
        return triggered ? Optional.of(new AlertTrigger(rule, currentVolume.toPlainString())) : Optional.empty();
    }
}
3e:T659,@Component
public class TradeConsumer {
    // constructor(ruleStore, evaluator, cooldown, publisher) ...

    @RabbitListener(queues = RabbitConfig.TRADES_QUEUE)
    public void onTrade(TradeEvent trade) {
        long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
        ruleStore.forSymbol(trade.symbol(), "PRICE_THRESHOLD").forEach(rule ->
            evaluator.evaluate(rule, trade).ifPresent(trigger -> {
                if (cooldown.shouldFire(rule.getId(), now)) {
                    publisher.publish(trigger.rule(), trigger.triggerValue());
                }
            })
        );
    }
}

@Component
public class CandleConsumer {
    // constructor(candleStore, ruleStore, percentChangeEvaluator, volumeSpikeEvaluator, cooldown, publisher) ...

    @RabbitListener(queues = RabbitConfig.CANDLES_QUEUE)
    public void onCandle(Candle1mEvent candle) {
        candleStore.add(candle);
        List<Candle1mEvent> recent = candleStore.recent(candle.symbol());
        long now = System.currentTimeMillis();

        ruleStore.forSymbol(candle.symbol(), "PERCENT_CHANGE").forEach(rule ->
            percentChangeEvaluator.evaluate(rule, recent).ifPresent(trigger -> {
                if (cooldown.shouldFire(rule.getId(), now)) publisher.publish(trigger.rule(), trigger.triggerValue());
            })
        );
        ruleStore.forSymbol(candle.symbol(), "VOLUME_SPIKE").forEach(rule ->
            volumeSpikeEvaluator.evaluate(rule, recent).ifPresent(trigger -> {
                if (cooldown.shouldFire(rule.getId(), now)) publisher.publish(trigger.rule(), trigger.triggerValue());
            })
        );
    }
}

import jakarta.persistence.*;

import java.time.OffsetDateTime;

@Entity
@Table(name = "alerts")
public class Alert {

    @Id
    private UUID id;

    @Column(name = "rule_id", nullable = false)
    private UUID ruleId;

    @Column(name = "tenant_id", nullable = false)
    private UUID tenantId;

    @Column(nullable = false, length = 20)
    private String symbol;

    @Column(name = "rule_type", nullable = false, length = 30)
    private String ruleType;

    @Column(name = "triggered_at", nullable = false)
    private OffsetDateTime triggeredAt;

    @Column(name = "trigger_value", nullable = false, length = 50)
    private String triggerValue;

    @Column(name = "webhook_url", nullable = false, length = 500)
    private String webhookUrl;

    @Column(nullable = false, length = 20)
    private String status = "PENDING";

    @CreationTimestamp
    @Column(name = "created_at", nullable = false, updatable = false)
    private OffsetDateTime createdAt;

    protected Alert() {}

    public Alert(UUID id, UUID ruleId, UUID tenantId, String symbol, String ruleType,
                 OffsetDateTime triggeredAt, String triggerValue, String webhookUrl) {
        this.id = id;
        this.ruleId = ruleId;
        this.tenantId = tenantId;
        this.symbol = symbol;
        this.ruleType = ruleType;
        this.triggeredAt = triggeredAt;
        this.triggerValue = triggerValue;
        this.webhookUrl = webhookUrl;
    }

    public void markDelivered() { this.status = "DELIVERED"; }
    public void markClientError() { this.status = "CLIENT_ERROR"; }
    public void markFailed() { this.status = "FAILED"; }

    public UUID getId() { return id; }
    public UUID getRuleId() { return ruleId; }
    public UUID getTenantId() { return tenantId; }
    public String getSymbol() { return symbol; }
    public String getRuleType() { return ruleType; }
    public OffsetDateTime getTriggeredAt() { return triggeredAt; }
    public String getTriggerValue() { return triggerValue; }
    public String getWebhookUrl() { return webhookUrl; }
    public String getStatus() { return status; }
    public OffsetDateTime getCreatedAt() { return createdAt; }
}

import org.springframework.amqp.core.*;
import org.springframework.amqp.support.converter.DefaultJackson2JavaTypeMapper;
import org.springframework.amqp.support.converter.Jackson2JsonMessageConverter;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;

@Configuration
public class RabbitConfig {

    // exchange nГ y do rule-engine khai bГЎo trЖ°б»ӣc (Chбә·ng 5); khai lбәЎi б»ҹ Д‘Гўy lГ  idempotent
    // vГ¬ cГ№ng thuб»ҷc tГӯnh (direct, durable, khГҙng auto-delete) вҖ” chб»ү Д‘б»ғ mб»ҹ queue riГӘng.
    public static final String ALERTS_EXCHANGE = "market-pulse.alerts";
    public static final String ALERTS_QUEUE = "alert-delivery.alerts";
    public static final String ALERTS_ROUTING_KEY = "alert";

    @Bean
    public DirectExchange alertsExchange() {
        return new DirectExchange(ALERTS_EXCHANGE, true, false);
    }

    @Bean
    public Queue alertsQueue() {
        return new Queue(ALERTS_QUEUE, true);
    }

    @Bean
    public Binding alertsBinding(Queue alertsQueue, DirectExchange alertsExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(alertsQueue).to(alertsExchange).with(ALERTS_ROUTING_KEY);
    }

    @Bean
    public Jackson2JsonMessageConverter jackson2JsonMessageConverter() {
        DefaultJackson2JavaTypeMapper typeMapper = new DefaultJackson2JavaTypeMapper();
        typeMapper.setTrustedPackages("com.marketpulse.*");
        Jackson2JsonMessageConverter converter = new Jackson2JsonMessageConverter();
        converter.setClassMapper(typeMapper);
        return converter;
    }
}
43:T785,package com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.client;

import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.http.MediaType;
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.function.client.WebClient;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.function.client.WebClientResponseException;

import java.time.Duration;

@Component
public class WebhookClient {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(WebhookClient.class);

    private final WebClient webClient;

    public WebhookClient(WebClient.Builder builder) {
        // khГҙng baseUrl cб»‘ Д‘б»Ӣnh: mб»—i alert cГі webhookUrl riГӘng cб»§a tenant
        this.webClient = builder.build();
    }

    public DeliveryAttemptResult send(String webhookUrl, WebhookPayload payload) {
        try {
            ResponseEntity<Void> response = webClient.post()
                    .uri(webhookUrl)
                    .contentType(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
                    .bodyValue(payload)
                    .retrieve()
                    .toBodilessEntity()
                    .timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(5))
                    .block();
            // retrieve() nГ©m WebClientResponseException б»ҹ nhГЎnh 4xx/5xx nГӘn tб»ӣi Д‘Гўy luГҙn lГ  2xx
            return DeliveryAttemptResult.success(response.getStatusCode().value());
        } catch (WebClientResponseException e) {
            int status = e.getStatusCode().value();
            if (e.getStatusCode().is4xxClientError()) {
                return DeliveryAttemptResult.clientError(status);
            }
            return DeliveryAttemptResult.serverError(status);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.warn("Webhook lб»—i kбәҝt nб»‘i/timeout: url={} error={}", webhookUrl, e.toString());
            return DeliveryAttemptResult.timeout();
        }
    }
}
44:Tf25,package com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.service;

import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.client.DeliveryAttemptResult;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.client.WebhookClient;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.client.WebhookPayload;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.domain.Alert;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.domain.AlertDeliveryAttempt;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.repository.AlertDeliveryAttemptRepository;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.repository.AlertRepository;
import com.marketpulse.common.event.AlertTriggeredEvent;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;

import java.time.OffsetDateTime;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class DeliveryService {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DeliveryService.class);

    // delay[i] = thб»қi gian chб»қ SAU KHI attempt (i+1) thбәҘt bбәЎi, trЖ°б»ӣc khi thб»ӯ attempt (i+2)
    // вҶ’ tб»•ng tб»‘i Д‘a 4 lбә§n gб»Қi webhook (1 lбә§n Д‘бә§u + 3 lбә§n thб»ӯ lбәЎi), Д‘Гәng R04: "retry sau 1s, 4s, 16s"
    private static final long[] RETRY_DELAYS_MS = {1000, 4000, 16000};
    private static final int MAX_ATTEMPTS = RETRY_DELAYS_MS.length + 1;

    private final AlertRepository alertRepository;
    private final AlertDeliveryAttemptRepository attemptRepository;
    private final WebhookClient webhookClient;

    public DeliveryService(AlertRepository alertRepository,
                            AlertDeliveryAttemptRepository attemptRepository,
                            WebhookClient webhookClient) {
        this.alertRepository = alertRepository;
        this.attemptRepository = attemptRepository;
        this.webhookClient = webhookClient;
    }

    public void deliver(AlertTriggeredEvent event) {
        UUID alertId = UUID.fromString(event.alertId());

        Optional<Alert> existing = alertRepository.findById(alertId);
        if (existing.isPresent() && !"PENDING".equals(existing.get().getStatus())) {
            log.info("Alert {} Д‘ГЈ б»ҹ trбәЎng thГЎi cuб»‘i ({}) вҖ” bб»Ҹ qua (RabbitMQ redeliver)",
                    alertId, existing.get().getStatus());
            return;
        }

        Alert alert = existing.orElseGet(() -> alertRepository.save(new Alert(
                alertId, UUID.fromString(event.ruleId()), UUID.fromString(event.tenantId()),
                event.symbol(), event.ruleType(), OffsetDateTime.parse(event.triggeredAt()),
                event.triggerValue(), event.webhookUrl())));

        WebhookPayload payload = new WebhookPayload(event.alertId(), event.ruleId(), event.symbol(),
                event.ruleType(), event.triggeredAt(), event.triggerValue());

        for (int attempt = 1; attempt <= MAX_ATTEMPTS; attempt++) {
            DeliveryAttemptResult result = webhookClient.send(event.webhookUrl(), payload);
            attemptRepository.save(new AlertDeliveryAttempt(alertId, attempt, result.httpStatus(), result.outcome()));
            log.info("Alert {} attempt {}/{}: {} (http={})",
                    alertId, attempt, MAX_ATTEMPTS, result.outcome(), result.httpStatus());

            if ("SUCCESS".equals(result.outcome())) {
                alert.markDelivered();
                alertRepository.save(alert);
                return;
            }
            if (!result.isRetryable()) {
                alert.markClientError();
                alertRepository.save(alert);
                return;
            }
            if (attempt < MAX_ATTEMPTS) {
                sleep(RETRY_DELAYS_MS[attempt - 1]);
            }
        }

        alert.markFailed();
        alertRepository.save(alert);
    }

    private void sleep(long ms) {
        try {
            Thread.sleep(ms);
        } catch (InterruptedException e) {
            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
        }
    }
}
45:T82f,package com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.controller;

import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.domain.Alert;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.dto.AlertAttemptResponse;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.dto.AlertDetailResponse;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.dto.AlertResponse;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.exception.AlertNotFoundException;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.repository.AlertDeliveryAttemptRepository;
import com.marketpulse.alertdelivery.repository.AlertRepository;
import org.springframework.data.domain.Page;
import org.springframework.data.domain.Pageable;
import org.springframework.data.domain.Sort;
import org.springframework.data.web.PageableDefault;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.UUID;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/alerts")
public class AlertController {

    private final AlertRepository alertRepository;
    private final AlertDeliveryAttemptRepository attemptRepository;

    public AlertController(AlertRepository alertRepository, AlertDeliveryAttemptRepository attemptRepository) {
        this.alertRepository = alertRepository;
        this.attemptRepository = attemptRepository;
    }

    @GetMapping
    public Page<AlertResponse> list(
            @RequestHeader("X-Tenant-Id") UUID tenantId,
            @PageableDefault(size = 20, sort = "createdAt", direction = Sort.Direction.DESC) Pageable pageable) {
        return alertRepository.findByTenantId(tenantId, pageable).map(AlertResponse::from);
    }

    @GetMapping("/{id}")
    public AlertDetailResponse detail(@PathVariable UUID id, @RequestHeader("X-Tenant-Id") UUID tenantId) {
        Alert alert = alertRepository.findById(id)
                .filter(a -> a.getTenantId().equals(tenantId))
                .orElseThrow(AlertNotFoundException::new);
        List<AlertAttemptResponse> attempts = attemptRepository.findByAlertIdOrderByAttemptNumberAsc(id).stream()
                .map(AlertAttemptResponse::from)
                .toList();
        return AlertDetailResponse.from(alert, attempts);
    }
}

import http.server, json

LOG = "/tmp/smoke-ch6-webhook-hits.ndjson"

class Handler(http.server.BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def do_POST(self):
        length = int(self.headers.get("Content-Length", 0))
        body = self.rfile.read(length)
        with open(LOG, "a") as f:
            f.write(json.dumps({"path": self.path, "body": body.decode("utf-8")}) + "\n")
        self.send_response(200 if self.path.startswith("/hook-200") else 500)
        self.end_headers()

    def log_message(self, fmt, *args):
        pass

http.server.HTTPServer(("0.0.0.0", 9999), Handler).serve_forever()

49:T533,package com.marketpulse.ruleengine.client;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.function.client.WebClient;

import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

@Component
public class QuotaClient {

    private final WebClient webClient;

    public QuotaClient(WebClient.Builder builder,
                       @Value("${billing.service.url}") String baseUrl) {
        this.webClient = builder.baseUrl(baseUrl).build();
    }

    /**
     * activeRules: billing khГҙng sб»ҹ hб»Ҝu bбәЈng rules (db-per-service) nГӘn khГҙng tб»ұ Д‘бәҝm Д‘Ж°б»Јc вҖ”
     * rule-engine Д‘бәҝm tб»« DB cб»§a chГӯnh mГ¬nh rб»“i truyб»Ғn qua, billing chб»ү so vб»ӣi giб»ӣi hбәЎn gГіi.
     * TrбәЈ empty nбәҝu billing chЖ°a phбәЈn hб»“i (timeout / connection refused).
     * Service xб»ӯ lГҪ fail-open: empty вҶ’ cho phГ©p tбәЎo rule.
     */
    public Optional<QuotaStatus> check(UUID tenantId, int activeRules) {
        return webClient.get()
                .uri("/internal/quota/{tenantId}?activeRules={activeRules}", tenantId, activeRules)
                .retrieve()
                .bodyToMono(QuotaStatus.class)
                .timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(2))
                .blockOptional();
    }
}
4a:T8b7,package com.marketpulse.billing.config;

import org.springframework.amqp.core.*;
import org.springframework.amqp.support.converter.DefaultJackson2JavaTypeMapper;
import org.springframework.amqp.support.converter.Jackson2JsonMessageConverter;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;

@Configuration
public class RabbitConfig {

    // exchange alerts: rule-engine khai gб»‘c (Chбә·ng 5) вҖ” billing khai lбәЎi idempotent (cГ№ng thuб»ҷc
    // tГӯnh) chб»ү Д‘б»ғ mб»ҹ queue RIГҠNG cб»§a mГ¬nh. billing + alert-delivery lГ  2 consumer Дҗб»ҳC Lбә¬P cб»§a
    // cГ№ng 1 exchange/routing-key: mб»—i bГӘn cГі queue riГӘng nГӘn Д‘б»Ғu nhбәӯn Д‘б»§ mб»Қi alert, khГҙng tranh nhau.
    public static final String ALERTS_EXCHANGE = "market-pulse.alerts";
    public static final String ALERTS_QUEUE = "billing.alerts";
    public static final String ALERTS_ROUTING_KEY = "alert";

    // exchange quota: rule-engine khai gб»‘c (Chбә·ng 5) Д‘б»ғ tб»ұ bind queue nghe; billing chб»ү PUBLISH
    // nГӘn khГҙng cбә§n khai queue, chб»ү cбә§n khai lбәЎi exchange (idempotent) Д‘б»ғ gб»ӯi vГ o.
    public static final String QUOTA_EXCHANGE = "market-pulse.quota";
    public static final String QUOTA_ROUTING_KEY = "quota.exceeded";

    @Bean
    public DirectExchange alertsExchange() {
        return new DirectExchange(ALERTS_EXCHANGE, true, false);
    }

    @Bean
    public Queue alertsQueue() {
        return new Queue(ALERTS_QUEUE, true);
    }

    @Bean
    public Binding alertsBinding(Queue alertsQueue, DirectExchange alertsExchange) {
        return BindingBuilder.bind(alertsQueue).to(alertsExchange).with(ALERTS_ROUTING_KEY);
    }

    @Bean
    public DirectExchange quotaExchange() {
        return new DirectExchange(QUOTA_EXCHANGE, true, false);
    }

    @Bean
    public Jackson2JsonMessageConverter jackson2JsonMessageConverter() {
        DefaultJackson2JavaTypeMapper typeMapper = new DefaultJackson2JavaTypeMapper();
        typeMapper.setTrustedPackages("com.marketpulse.*");
        Jackson2JsonMessageConverter converter = new Jackson2JsonMessageConverter();
        converter.setClassMapper(typeMapper);
        return converter;
    }
}
4b:T934,package com.marketpulse.billing.client;

import com.github.benmanes.caffeine.cache.Cache;
import com.github.benmanes.caffeine.cache.Caffeine;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.function.client.WebClient;

import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

/**
 * Resolve giб»ӣi hбәЎn gГіi (maxRules/maxAlertsPm) cб»§a tenant qua identity вҖ” billing khГҙng cГі DB
 * riГӘng cho plan (db-per-service: identity lГ  chб»§ sб»ҹ hб»Ҝu duy nhбәҘt cб»§a tenant+plan).
 * Cache 60s (Caffeine, giб»‘ng ApiKeyAuthFilter): plan hiбәҝm khi Д‘б»•i, khГҙng cбә§n tra mб»—i request.
 */
@Component
public class TenantPlanClient {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TenantPlanClient.class);

    private final WebClient webClient;
    private final Cache<UUID, TenantPlan> cache;

    public TenantPlanClient(WebClient.Builder builder, @Value("${identity.service.url}") String baseUrl) {
        this.webClient = builder.baseUrl(baseUrl).build();
        this.cache = Caffeine.newBuilder()
                .expireAfterWrite(60, TimeUnit.SECONDS)
                .maximumSize(10_000)
                .build();
    }

    /** Empty nбәҝu identity khГҙng phбәЈn hб»“i hoбә·c tenant khГҙng tб»“n tбәЎi вҖ” caller tб»ұ quyбәҝt fail-open. */
    public Optional<TenantPlan> get(UUID tenantId) {
        TenantPlan cached = cache.getIfPresent(tenantId);
        if (cached != null) {
            return Optional.of(cached);
        }
        try {
            InternalTenantResponse resp = webClient.get()
                    .uri("/internal/tenants/{tenantId}", tenantId)
                    .retrieve()
                    .bodyToMono(InternalTenantResponse.class)
                    .timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(2))
                    .block();
            TenantPlan plan = new TenantPlan(resp.maxRules(), resp.maxAlertsPm());
            cache.put(tenantId, plan);
            return Optional.of(plan);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.warn("identity unavailable, khГҙng resolve Д‘Ж°б»Јc plan cho tenant {}: {}", tenantId, e.getMessage());
            return Optional.empty();
        }
    }
}
4c:T5b0,package com.marketpulse.billing.repository;

import com.marketpulse.billing.domain.UsagePeriod;
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.JpaRepository;
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.Modifying;
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.Query;
import org.springframework.data.repository.query.Param;
import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

public interface UsagePeriodRepository extends JpaRepository<UsagePeriod, UUID> {

    Optional<UsagePeriod> findByTenantIdAndPeriod(UUID tenantId, String period);

    /**
     * INSERT..ON CONFLICT thay vГ¬ SELECT-rб»“i-UPDATE: trГЎnh race khi 2 alert cб»§a cГ№ng tenant
     * Д‘бәҝn gбә§n nhЖ° Д‘б»“ng thб»қi вҖ” 2 request riГӘng biб»Үt cГ№ng "thбәҘy" dГІng chЖ°a tб»“n tбәЎi rб»“i cГ№ng INSERT
     * sбәҪ vб»Ў unique constraint (tenant_id, period); upsert nguyГӘn tб»ӯ б»ҹ tбә§ng DB loбәЎi bб»Ҹ khбәЈ nДғng Д‘Гі.
     */
    @Transactional
    @Modifying
    @Query(value = """
            INSERT INTO usage_periods (id, tenant_id, period, alerts_fired, updated_at)
            VALUES (gen_random_uuid(), :tenantId, :period, 1, now())
            ON CONFLICT (tenant_id, period)
            DO UPDATE SET alerts_fired = usage_periods.alerts_fired + 1, updated_at = now()
            """, nativeQuery = true)
    void incrementAlertsFired(@Param("tenantId") UUID tenantId, @Param("period") String period);
}
4d:T85d,package com.marketpulse.billing.service;

import com.marketpulse.billing.client.TenantPlan;
import com.marketpulse.billing.client.TenantPlanClient;
import com.marketpulse.billing.domain.UsagePeriod;
import com.marketpulse.billing.repository.UsagePeriodRepository;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;

import java.time.YearMonth;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class UsageService {

    private final UsagePeriodRepository usagePeriodRepository;
    private final TenantPlanClient tenantPlanClient;
    private final QuotaEventPublisher quotaEventPublisher;

    public UsageService(UsagePeriodRepository usagePeriodRepository,
                         TenantPlanClient tenantPlanClient,
                         QuotaEventPublisher quotaEventPublisher) {
        this.usagePeriodRepository = usagePeriodRepository;
        this.tenantPlanClient = tenantPlanClient;
        this.quotaEventPublisher = quotaEventPublisher;
    }

    /** TДғng Д‘бәҝm alert Д‘ГЈ bбәҜn trong thГЎng; nбәҝu vЖ°б»Јt max_alerts_pm cб»§a gГіi вҶ’ phГЎt QuotaExceededEvent. */
    public void recordAlertFired(UUID tenantId) {
        String period = currentPeriod();
        usagePeriodRepository.incrementAlertsFired(tenantId, period);
        int current = alertsFiredInCurrentPeriod(tenantId, period);

        tenantPlanClient.get(tenantId).ifPresent(plan -> {
            if (current > plan.maxAlertsPm()) {
                quotaEventPublisher.publishAlertsExceeded(tenantId, current, plan.maxAlertsPm());
            }
        });
    }

    public int alertsFiredInCurrentPeriod(UUID tenantId) {
        return alertsFiredInCurrentPeriod(tenantId, currentPeriod());
    }

    public Optional<TenantPlan> planFor(UUID tenantId) {
        return tenantPlanClient.get(tenantId);
    }

    private int alertsFiredInCurrentPeriod(UUID tenantId, String period) {
        return usagePeriodRepository.findByTenantIdAndPeriod(tenantId, period)
                .map(UsagePeriod::getAlertsFired)
                .orElse(0);
    }

    private String currentPeriod() {
        return YearMonth.now().toString();
    }
}
4e:T4b8,package com.marketpulse.billing.service;

import com.marketpulse.billing.config.RabbitConfig;
import com.marketpulse.common.event.QuotaExceededEvent;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.amqp.rabbit.core.RabbitTemplate;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.time.OffsetDateTime;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.util.UUID;

@Component
public class QuotaEventPublisher {

    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(QuotaEventPublisher.class);

    private final RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate;

    public QuotaEventPublisher(RabbitTemplate rabbitTemplate) {
        this.rabbitTemplate = rabbitTemplate;
    }

    public void publishAlertsExceeded(UUID tenantId, int currentCount, int limit) {
        QuotaExceededEvent event = new QuotaExceededEvent(
                tenantId.toString(), "ALERTS", currentCount, limit,
                OffsetDateTime.now(ZoneOffset.UTC).toString());
        rabbitTemplate.convertAndSend(RabbitConfig.QUOTA_EXCHANGE, RabbitConfig.QUOTA_ROUTING_KEY, event);
        log.info("Quota alerts vЖ°б»Јt mб»©c: tenant={} current={} limit={}", tenantId, currentCount, limit);
    }
}
4f:T739,package com.marketpulse.billing.controller;

import com.marketpulse.billing.client.TenantPlan;
import com.marketpulse.billing.dto.QuotaStatusResponse;
import com.marketpulse.billing.service.UsageService;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PathVariable;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestParam;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;

@RestController
public class InternalQuotaController {

    private final UsageService usageService;

    public InternalQuotaController(UsageService usageService) {
        this.usageService = usageService;
    }

    // Chб»ү dГ№ng nб»ҷi bб»ҷ Docker network вҖ” rule-engine gб»Қi khi tбәЎo rule (ADR-003, rule quota sync).
    // activeRules: rule-engine tб»ұ Д‘бәҝm rб»“i truyб»Ғn vГ o (billing khГҙng sб»ҹ hб»Ҝu bбәЈng rules).
    @GetMapping("/internal/quota/{tenantId}")
    public QuotaStatusResponse getQuota(@PathVariable UUID tenantId, @RequestParam int activeRules) {
        int alertsThisMonth = usageService.alertsFiredInCurrentPeriod(tenantId);
        Optional<TenantPlan> planOpt = usageService.planFor(tenantId);

        if (planOpt.isEmpty()) {
            // identity khГҙng phбәЈn hб»“i: fail-open вҖ” khГҙng exceed, rule-engine (cЕ©ng fail-open) tб»ұ quyбәҝt tiбәҝp
            return new QuotaStatusResponse(activeRules, 0, alertsThisMonth, 0, false, false);
        }

        TenantPlan plan = planOpt.get();
        boolean rulesExceeded = activeRules >= plan.maxRules();
        boolean alertsExceeded = alertsThisMonth > plan.maxAlertsPm();
        return new QuotaStatusResponse(
                activeRules, plan.maxRules(), alertsThisMonth, plan.maxAlertsPm(),
                rulesExceeded, alertsExceeded);
    }
}
50:T43d,package com.marketpulse.billing.controller;

import com.marketpulse.billing.client.TenantPlan;
import com.marketpulse.billing.dto.UsageResponse;
import com.marketpulse.billing.service.UsageService;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestHeader;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

import java.util.UUID;

@RestController
@RequestMapping("/api/v1/usage")
public class UsageController {

    private final UsageService usageService;

    public UsageController(UsageService usageService) {
        this.usageService = usageService;
    }

    @GetMapping
    public UsageResponse getUsage(@RequestHeader("X-Tenant-Id") UUID tenantId) {
        int alertsFired = usageService.alertsFiredInCurrentPeriod(tenantId);
        TenantPlan plan = usageService.planFor(tenantId).orElse(new TenantPlan(0, 0));
        return new UsageResponse(usageService.currentPeriod(), alertsFired, plan.maxAlertsPm(), plan.maxRules());
    }
}

# smoke-ch7.sh вҖ” Milestone Chбә·ng 7: billing вҖ” rule quota (sync) + alert quota (event-driven).
# YГӘu cбә§u: rabbitmq + identity + rule-engine + billing (+ 3 DB) Д‘ang chбәЎy.

check() {
    local label="$1" got="$2" want="$3"
    if [ "$got" = "$want" ]; then echo "PASS  ${label}"; PASS=$((PASS + 1))
    else echo "FAIL  ${label}  (got=${got}, want=${want})"; FAIL=$((FAIL + 1)); fi
}

        -H "content-type: application/json" -d "${payload}" >/dev/null 2>&1
}

53:T619,const BASE_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_GATEWAY_URL ?? 'http://localhost:8080';
const API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY = 'mp_api_key';

export class ApiError extends Error {
  status: number;
  constructor(status: number, message: string) {
    super(message);
    this.status = status;
  }
}

export function getStoredApiKey(): string | null {
  return localStorage.getItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY);
}

export function setStoredApiKey(key: string) {
  localStorage.setItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY, key);
}

export function clearStoredApiKey() {
  localStorage.removeItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY);
}

async function request<T>(path: string, options: RequestInit = {}): Promise<T> {
  const apiKey = getStoredApiKey();
  const headers = new Headers(options.headers);
  headers.set('Content-Type', 'application/json');
  if (apiKey) headers.set('X-API-Key', apiKey);

  const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}${path}`, { ...options, headers });

  if (!res.ok) {
    let message = res.statusText;
    try {
      const body = await res.json();
      message = body.error ?? message;
    } catch {
      // body khГҙng phбәЈi JSON (vd: lб»—i hбәЎ tбә§ng) вҖ” giб»Ҝ statusText
    }
    throw new ApiError(res.status, message);
  }

  if (res.status === 204) return undefined as T;
  return res.json();
}

export const api = {
  get: <T>(path: string) => request<T>(path),
  post: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) =>
    request<T>(path, { method: 'POST', body: body !== undefined ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined }),
  delete: (path: string) => request<void>(path, { method: 'DELETE' }),
};

export default function LoginPage() {
  const { isAuthenticated, login } = useAuth();
  const [key, setKey] = useState('');
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [checking, setChecking] = useState(false);

  if (isAuthenticated) return <Navigate to="/" replace />;

  async function handleSubmit(e: FormEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    const trimmed = key.trim();
    if (!trimmed) return;

    setChecking(true);
    setError(null);
    // xГЎc thб»ұc ngay bбәұng 1 call nhбә№ вҖ” trГЎnh "Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp" xong mб»ӣi bГЎo sai key б»ҹ trang sau
    setStoredApiKey(trimmed);
    try {
      await api.get<Usage>('/api/v1/usage');
      login(trimmed);
    } catch {
      clearStoredApiKey();
      setError('API key khГҙng hб»Јp lб»Ү hoбә·c Д‘ГЈ bб»Ӣ thu hб»“i.');
    } finally {
      setChecking(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="login-screen">
      <form className="login-card" onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
        <h1>Market Pulse</h1>
        <p className="login-subtitle">Nhбәӯp API key Д‘б»ғ vГ o dashboard.</p>
        <input
          type="text"
          value={key}
          onChange={(e) => setKey(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="mp_..."
          autoFocus
        />
        {error && <p className="login-error">{error}</p>}
        <button type="submit" disabled={checking || !key.trim()}>
          {checking ? 'Дҗang kiб»ғm tra...' : 'ДҗДғng nhбәӯp'}
        </button>
        <p className="login-hint">
          Demo: <code>demo-key-acme-2026</code> (tenant Acme Corp, gГіi starter)
        </p>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
}
57:T73f,const BASE_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_GATEWAY_URL ?? 'http://localhost:8080';
const API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY = 'mp_api_key';

/** client.ts lГ  module thuбә§n, khГҙng import React вҖ” bГЎo lб»—i auth qua event Д‘б»ғ AuthProvider tб»ұ lбәҜng nghe. */
export const AUTH_ERROR_EVENT = 'mp:auth-error';

export class ApiError extends Error {
  status: number;
  constructor(status: number, message: string) {
    super(message);
    this.status = status;
  }
}

export function getStoredApiKey(): string | null {
  return localStorage.getItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY);
}

export function setStoredApiKey(key: string) {
  localStorage.setItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY, key);
}

export function clearStoredApiKey() {
  localStorage.removeItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY);
}

async function request<T>(path: string, options: RequestInit = {}): Promise<T> {
  const apiKey = getStoredApiKey();
  const headers = new Headers(options.headers);
  headers.set('Content-Type', 'application/json');
  if (apiKey) headers.set('X-API-Key', apiKey);

  const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}${path}`, { ...options, headers });

  if (!res.ok) {
    let message = res.statusText;
    try {
      const body = await res.json();
      message = body.error ?? message;
    } catch {
      // body khГҙng phбәЈi JSON (vd: lб»—i hбәЎ tбә§ng) вҖ” giб»Ҝ statusText
    }
    if (res.status === 401) {
      clearStoredApiKey();
      window.dispatchEvent(new Event(AUTH_ERROR_EVENT));
    }
    throw new ApiError(res.status, message);
  }

  if (res.status === 204) return undefined as T;
  return res.json();
}

export const api = {
  get: <T>(path: string) => request<T>(path),
  post: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) =>
    request<T>(path, { method: 'POST', body: body !== undefined ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined }),
  delete: (path: string) => request<void>(path, { method: 'DELETE' }),
};
58:T4f6,import { createContext, useCallback, useContext, useEffect, useState, type ReactNode } from 'react';
import { AUTH_ERROR_EVENT, clearStoredApiKey, getStoredApiKey, setStoredApiKey } from '../api/client';

interface AuthContextValue {
  isAuthenticated: boolean;
  login: (key: string) => void;
  logout: () => void;
}

const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextValue | null>(null);

export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const [isAuthenticated, setIsAuthenticated] = useState(() => getStoredApiKey() !== null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleAuthError = () => setIsAuthenticated(false);
    window.addEventListener(AUTH_ERROR_EVENT, handleAuthError);
    return () => window.removeEventListener(AUTH_ERROR_EVENT, handleAuthError);
  }, []);

  const login = useCallback((key: string) => {
    setStoredApiKey(key);
    setIsAuthenticated(true);
  }, []);

  const logout = useCallback(() => {
    clearStoredApiKey();
    setIsAuthenticated(false);
  }, []);

  return <AuthContext.Provider value={{ isAuthenticated, login, logout }}>{children}</AuthContext.Provider>;
}

export function useAuth() {
  const ctx = useContext(AuthContext);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error('useAuth phбәЈi dГ№ng trong AuthProvider');
  return ctx;
}
59:T549,import type { ReactNode } from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter, Navigate, Route, Routes } from 'react-router-dom';
import { AuthProvider, useAuth } from './auth/AuthContext';
import Layout from './components/Layout';
import LoginPage from './pages/LoginPage';
import RulesPage from './pages/RulesPage';
import AlertsPage from './pages/AlertsPage';
import KeysPage from './pages/KeysPage';
import UsagePage from './pages/UsagePage';

function RequireAuth({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const { isAuthenticated } = useAuth();
  if (!isAuthenticated) return <Navigate to="/login" replace />;
  return <>{children}</>;
}

export default function App() {
  return (
    <AuthProvider>
      <BrowserRouter>
        <Routes>
          <Route path="/login" element={<LoginPage />} />
          <Route
            path="/"
            element={
              <RequireAuth>
                <Layout />
              </RequireAuth>
            }
          >
            <Route index element={<Navigate to="/rules" replace />} />
            <Route path="rules" element={<RulesPage />} />
            <Route path="alerts" element={<AlertsPage />} />
            <Route path="keys" element={<KeysPage />} />
            <Route path="usage" element={<UsagePage />} />
          </Route>
        </Routes>
      </BrowserRouter>
    </AuthProvider>
  );
}
5a:T1072,import { useEffect, useState, type FormEvent } from 'react';
import { api, ApiError } from '../api/client';
import type { ApiKeySummary, CreateKeyResponse } from '../api/types';

export default function KeysPage() {
  const [keys, setKeys] = useState<ApiKeySummary[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [label, setLabel] = useState('');
  const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false);
  // key thГҙ chб»ү giб»Ҝ trong state (khГҙng lЖ°u Д‘Гўu khГЎc) вҖ” mбәҘt khi rб»қi trang hoбә·c reload, Д‘Гәng ГҪ "chб»ү hiб»Үn 1 lбә§n"
  const [justCreated, setJustCreated] = useState<CreateKeyResponse | null>(null);

  async function load() {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const data = await api.get<ApiKeySummary[]>('/api/v1/keys');
      setKeys(data);
    } catch (e) {
      setError(e instanceof ApiError ? e.message : 'KhГҙng tбәЈi Д‘Ж°б»Јc danh sГЎch key.');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    load();
  }, []);

  async function handleCreate(e: FormEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    setCreating(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const created = await api.post<CreateKeyResponse>('/api/v1/keys', {
        label: label.trim() || null,
      });
      setJustCreated(created);
      setLabel('');
      await load();
    } catch (e) {
      setError(e instanceof ApiError ? e.message : 'TбәЎo key thбәҘt bбәЎi.');
    } finally {
      setCreating(false);
    }
  }

  async function handleRevoke(id: string) {
    try {
      await api.delete(`/api/v1/keys/${id}`);
      await load();
    } catch (e) {
      setError(e instanceof ApiError ? e.message : 'Thu hб»“i key thбәҘt bбәЎi.');
    }
  }

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="page-header">
        <h1>API Keys</h1>

const RULE_TYPE_LABELS: Record<RuleType, string> = {
  PRICE_THRESHOLD: 'NgЖ°б»Ўng giГЎ',
  PERCENT_CHANGE: '% thay Д‘б»•i',
  VOLUME_SPIKE: 'Дҗб»ҷt biбәҝn khб»‘i lЖ°б»Јng',

function friendlyError(e: unknown): string {
  if (e instanceof ApiError) {
    if (e.body?.error === 'QUOTA_EXCEEDED_RULES') {
      return `ДҗГЈ Д‘бәЎt giб»ӣi hбәЎn rule cб»§a gГіi (${e.body.current}/${e.body.limit}) вҖ” xoГЎ bб»ӣt rule hoбә·c nГўng gГіi.`;
    }
    return e.message;
  }
  return 'CГі lб»—i xбәЈy ra.';
}

export default function RulesPage() {
  const [rules, setRules] = useState<Rule[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false);

  const [symbol, setSymbol] = useState('BTCUSDT');
  const [type, setType] = useState<RuleType>('PRICE_THRESHOLD');
  const [webhookUrl, setWebhookUrl] = useState('https://example.com/hook');
  const [threshold, setThreshold] = useState('50000');
  const [direction, setDirection] = useState('BELOW');
  const [percent, setPercent] = useState('5');
  const [windowMinutes, setWindowMinutes] = useState('5');
  const [multiplier, setMultiplier] = useState('3');

  async function load() {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      setRules(await api.get<Rule[]>('/api/v1/rules'));
    } catch (e) {
      setError(friendlyError(e));
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    load();
  }, []);

  function buildParams(): Record<string, string> {
    switch (type) {
      case 'PRICE_THRESHOLD':
        return { threshold, direction };
      case 'PERCENT_CHANGE':
        return { percent, windowMinutes, direction: direction === 'BELOW' ? 'DOWN' : 'UP' };
      case 'VOLUME_SPIKE':
        return { multiplier };
    }
  }

  async function handleCreate(e: FormEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    setCreating(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      await api.post('/api/v1/rules', { symbol, type, params: buildParams(), webhookUrl });
      await load();
    } catch (e) {
      setError(friendlyError(e));
    } finally {
      setCreating(false);
    }
  }

  async function handleDelete(id: string) {
    try {
      await api.delete(`/api/v1/rules/${id}`);
      await load();
    } catch (e) {
      setError(friendlyError(e));
    }
  }

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="page-header">
        <h1>Rules</h1>
      </div>

      {error && <div className="error-banner">{error}</div>}

      <form className="form-card" onSubmit={handleCreate}>
        <h3>TбәЎo rule mб»ӣi</h3>
        <div className="form-row">
          <label htmlFor="symbol">Symbol</label>
          <input id="symbol" value={symbol} onChange={(e) => setSymbol(e.target.value.toUpperCase())} required />
        </div>
        <div className="form-row">
          <label htmlFor="type">LoбәЎi rule</label>
          <select id="type" value={type} onChange={(e) => setType(e.target.value as RuleType)}>
            {Object.entries(RULE_TYPE_LABELS).map(([value, label]) => (
              <option key={value} value={value}>{label}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        {type === 'PRICE_THRESHOLD' && (
          <>
            <div className="form-row">
              <label htmlFor="threshold">NgЖ°б»Ўng giГЎ</label>
              <input id="threshold" type="number" value={threshold} onChange={(e) => setThreshold(e.target.value)} required />
            </div>
            <div className="form-row">
              <label htmlFor="direction">HЖ°б»ӣng</label>
              <select id="direction" value={direction} onChange={(e) => setDirection(e.target.value)}>
                <option value="BELOW">Xuб»‘ng dЖ°б»ӣi (BELOW)</option>
                <option value="ABOVE">VЖ°б»Јt lГӘn (ABOVE)</option>
              </select>
            </div>
          </>

5c:T869,const BASE_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_GATEWAY_URL ?? 'http://localhost:8080';
const API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY = 'mp_api_key';

/** client.ts lГ  module thuбә§n, khГҙng import React вҖ” bГЎo lб»—i auth qua event Д‘б»ғ AuthProvider tб»ұ lбәҜng nghe. */
export const AUTH_ERROR_EVENT = 'mp:auth-error';

export class ApiError extends Error {
  status: number;
  /** body lб»—i gб»‘c (vd: {error, limit, current} cб»§a QUOTA_EXCEEDED_RULES) вҖ” caller tб»ұ Д‘б»Қc thГӘm field cбә§n. */
  body: Record<string, unknown> | null;
  constructor(status: number, message: string, body: Record<string, unknown> | null = null) {
    super(message);
    this.status = status;
    this.body = body;
  }
}

export function getStoredApiKey(): string | null {
  return localStorage.getItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY);
}

export function setStoredApiKey(key: string) {
  localStorage.setItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY, key);
}

export function clearStoredApiKey() {
  localStorage.removeItem(API_KEY_STORAGE_KEY);
}

async function request<T>(path: string, options: RequestInit = {}): Promise<T> {
  const apiKey = getStoredApiKey();
  const headers = new Headers(options.headers);
  headers.set('Content-Type', 'application/json');
  if (apiKey) headers.set('X-API-Key', apiKey);

  const res = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}${path}`, { ...options, headers });

  if (!res.ok) {
    let message = res.statusText;
    let body: Record<string, unknown> | null = null;
    try {
      body = await res.json();
      message = (body?.error as string) ?? message;
    } catch {
      // body khГҙng phбәЈi JSON (vd: lб»—i hбәЎ tбә§ng) вҖ” giб»Ҝ statusText
    }
    if (res.status === 401) {
      clearStoredApiKey();
      window.dispatchEvent(new Event(AUTH_ERROR_EVENT));
    }
    throw new ApiError(res.status, message, body);
  }

  if (res.status === 204) return undefined as T;
  return res.json();
}

export const api = {
  get: <T>(path: string) => request<T>(path),
  post: <T>(path: string, body?: unknown) =>
    request<T>(path, { method: 'POST', body: body !== undefined ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined }),
  delete: (path: string) => request<void>(path, { method: 'DELETE' }),
};

export default function AlertsPage() {

  const [pageNumber, setPageNumber] = useState(0);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const [detailLoading, setDetailLoading] = useState(false);

  async function load(pageNum: number, silent = false) {
    if (!silent) setError(null);
    try {
      const data = await api.get<PageResponse<AlertSummary>>(`/api/v1/alerts?page=${pageNum}&size=20`);
      setPage(data);
    } catch (e) {
      if (!silent) setError(e instanceof ApiError ? e.message : 'KhГҙng tбәЈi Д‘Ж°б»Јc alert.');
    }
  }

    load(pageNumber);
  }, [pageNumber]);

  useEffect(() => {

    return () => clearInterval(id);
  }, [pageNumber]);

      setExpandedId(null);
      setDetail(null);
      return;

      setError(e instanceof ApiError ? e.message : 'KhГҙng tбәЈi Д‘Ж°б»Јc chi tiбәҝt alert.');
    } finally {
      setDetailLoading(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="page-header">
        <h1>Alerts</h1>
      </div>

      {error && <div className="error-banner">{error}</div>}

      {!page ? (
        <p>Дҗang tбәЈi...</p>
      ) : page.content.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="empty-state">ChЖ°a cГі alert nГ o.</div>
      ) : (
        <>
          <table>
            <thead>
              <tr>
                <th>Symbol</th>
                <th>LoбәЎi rule</th>
                <th>GiГЎ trб»Ӣ</th>
                <th>TrбәЎng thГЎi</th>
                <th>Trigger lГәc</th>
                <th></th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {page.content.map((a) => (
                <Fragment key={a.id}>
                  <tr onClick={() => toggleExpand(a.id)} style={{ cursor: 'pointer' }}>
                    <td>{a.symbol}</td>
                    <td>{a.ruleType}</td>
                    <td>{a.triggerValue}</td>
                    <td><span className={`badge status-${a.status.toLowerCase()}`}>{a.status}</span></td>
                    <td>{new Date(a.triggeredAt).toLocaleString('vi-VN')}</td>
                    <td>{expandedId === a.id ? 'в–І' : 'в–ј'}</td>

                    <tr>
                      <td colSpan={6} style={{ background: 'var(--bg-subtle)' }}>
                        {detailLoading ? (
                          <p>Дҗang tбәЈi chi tiбәҝt...</p>

                                <th>HTTP status</th>
                                <th>Kбәҝt quбәЈ</th>

                                </tr>
                              ))}
                            </tbody>
                          </table>
                        ) : null}
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  )}
                </Fragment>
              ))}
            </tbody>
          </table>

          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 12, marginTop: 16, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            <button type="button" disabled={page.number === 0} onClick={() => setPageNumber((p) => p - 1)}>
              вҶҗ TrЖ°б»ӣc

            </button>

5e:T7dc,import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { api, ApiError } from '../api/client';
import type { Rule, Usage } from '../api/types';

function ProgressStat({ label, current, max }: { label: string; current: number; max: number }) {
  const pct = max > 0 ? Math.min((current / max) * 100, 100) : 0;
  const over = current >= max;
  return (
    <div className="form-card" style={{ maxWidth: 480 }}>
      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
        <strong>{label}</strong>
        <span>{current} / {max}</span>
      </div>
      <div className="progress-bar">
        <div className={`progress-bar-fill${over ? ' over-limit' : ''}`} style={{ width: `${pct}%` }} />
      </div>
      {over && <p style={{ color: 'var(--danger)', margin: 0 }}>ДҗГЈ Д‘бәЎt giб»ӣi hбәЎn gГіi.</p>}
    </div>
  );
}

export default function UsagePage() {
  const [usage, setUsage] = useState<Usage | null>(null);
  const [activeRules, setActiveRules] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      setError(null);
      try {
        const [usageData, rules] = await Promise.all([
          api.get<Usage>('/api/v1/usage'),
          api.get<Rule[]>('/api/v1/rules'),
        ]);
        setUsage(usageData);
        setActiveRules(rules.filter((r) => r.status === 'ACTIVE').length);
      } catch (e) {
        setError(e instanceof ApiError ? e.message : 'KhГҙng tбәЈi Д‘Ж°б»Јc usage.');
      }
    }
    load();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <div className="page-header">
        <h1>Usage</h1>
      </div>

      {error && <div className="error-banner">{error}</div>}

      {usage && activeRules !== null && (
        <>
          <ProgressStat label="Active rules" current={activeRules} max={usage.maxRules} />
          <ProgressStat label={`Alerts thГЎng ${usage.period}`} current={usage.alertsFired} max={usage.maxAlertsPerMonth} />
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

# load-test.sh вҖ” Chбә·ng 9: replay б»ҹ multiplier cho trЖ°б»ӣc, theo dГөi rule-engine.trades queue depth.
# CГЎch dГ№ng: bash scripts/load-test.sh <multiplier> [thoi-gian-giay=60] [REPLAY_FILE]
# YГӘu cбә§u: rabbitmq + market-feed + aggregation + rule-engine Д‘ang chбәЎy; Д‘ГЈ cГі file record
#          (FEED_MODE=record trЖ°б»ӣc Д‘Гі) trong volume market-feed-data вҖ” nбәҝu khГҙng truyб»Ғn tham sб»‘ 3,
#          script tб»ұ lбәҘy file .ndjson mб»ӣi nhбәҘt trong volume.
# TiГӘu chГӯ "gГЈy" (OQ5, architecture.md В§7.1): rule-engine.trades > 5,000 msg tбәЎi bбәҘt kб»і thб»қi Д‘iб»ғm nГ o.

set -uo pipefail

MULTIPLIER="${1:-3}"
DURATION="${2:-60}"
REPLAY_FILE_ARG="${3:-}"
COMPOSE_FILE="${COMPOSE_FILE:-infra/docker-compose.yml}"
RMQ_USER="${RABBITMQ_USER:-market_pulse}"
RMQ_PASS="${RABBITMQ_PASSWORD:-change_me}"
RMQ_API="http://localhost:15672/api"
QUEUE="rule-engine.trades"
BREAK_THRESHOLD=5000
INTERVAL=5

REPLAY_FILE="${REPLAY_FILE_ARG}"
if [ -z "${REPLAY_FILE}" ]; then
    REPLAY_FILE=$(docker run --rm -v infra_market-feed-data:/data alpine sh -c "ls -t /data/*.ndjson 2>/dev/null | head -1")
    if [ -z "${REPLAY_FILE}" ]; then
        echo "FAIL KhГҙng tГ¬m thбәҘy file record nГ o trong volume market-feed-data."
        echo "     ChбәЎy trЖ°б»ӣc: FEED_MODE=record docker compose -f ${COMPOSE_FILE} up -d market-feed"
        exit 1
    fi
fi

echo "=== Load-test: replay x${MULTIPLIER}, theo dГөi ${DURATION}s, ngЖ°б»Ўng gГЈy = ${BREAK_THRESHOLD} msg (OQ5) ==="
echo "File nguб»“n: ${REPLAY_FILE}"
echo ""

FEED_MODE=replay REPLAY_FILE="${REPLAY_FILE}" REPLAY_MULTIPLIER="${MULTIPLIER}" REPLAY_LOOP=true \
    docker compose -f "${COMPOSE_FILE}" up -d --force-recreate market-feed >/dev/null 2>&1

max_depth=0
broken=false
iterations=$((DURATION / INTERVAL))
for i in $(seq 1 "${iterations}"); do
    sleep "${INTERVAL}"
    depth=$(curl -s -u "${RMQ_USER}:${RMQ_PASS}" "${RMQ_API}/queues/%2F/${QUEUE}" | \
        python3 -c "import sys,json; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get('messages',0))" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
    echo "t=$((i * INTERVAL))s  ${QUEUE} depth=${depth}"
    if [ "${depth}" -gt "${max_depth}" ] 2>/dev/null; then max_depth=${depth}; fi
    if [ "${depth}" -gt "${BREAK_THRESHOLD}" ] 2>/dev/null; then broken=true; fi
done

echo ""
echo "=== Kбәҝt quбәЈ: multiplier=x${MULTIPLIER}  max_depth_quan_sГЎt=${max_depth} ==="
if [ "${broken}" = true ]; then
    echo "GГғY вҖ” depth vЖ°б»Јt ${BREAK_THRESHOLD} msg (tiГӘu chГӯ OQ5 chГӯnh)."
    exit 1
else
    echo "PASS вҖ” depth khГҙng vЖ°б»Јt ${BREAK_THRESHOLD} msg trong ${DURATION}s quan sГЎt."
    exit 0
fi

62:T1511,#!/usr/bin/env bash
# smoke-full.sh вҖ” Milestone Chбә·ng 10: docker compose --profile full, verify TOГҖN Bб»ҳ hб»Ү + 1 vГІng
# nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt Д‘бә§u-cuб»‘i (tбәЎo key вҶ’ tбәЎo rule вҶ’ alert tб»ұ trigger tб»« trade Binance THбә¬T вҶ’ DELIVERED).
# KhГҙng publish event giбәЈ lбәӯp вҖ” dб»ұa hoГ n toГ n vГ o market-feed FEED_MODE=live Д‘ang chбәЎy thбәӯt.
# CГЎch chбәЎy: bash scripts/smoke-full.sh (yГӘu cбә§u Д‘ГЈ `docker compose --profile full up -d`)

set -uo pipefail

COMPOSE_FILE="${COMPOSE_FILE:-infra/docker-compose.yml}"
GATEWAY_URL="${GATEWAY_URL:-http://localhost:8080}"
IDENTITY_URL="${IDENTITY_URL:-http://localhost:8081}"
TENANT_ID="${TENANT_ID:-00000000-0000-0000-0001-000000000001}"
PASS=0
FAIL=0

check() {
    local label="$1" got="$2" want="$3"
    if [ "$got" = "$want" ]; then echo "PASS  ${label}"; PASS=$((PASS + 1))
    else echo "FAIL  ${label}  (got=${got}, want=${want})"; FAIL=$((FAIL + 1)); fi
}

echo "=== Smoke test Chбә·ng 10 вҖ” profile full, trб»Қn hб»Ү + 1 vГІng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt ==="
echo ""

# в”Җв”Җ TC1-9: healthcheck toГ n bб»ҷ service cГі healthcheck в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
for svc in gateway identity market-feed aggregation rule-engine alert-delivery billing \
           identity-db aggregation-db rule-engine-db alert-delivery-db billing-db rabbitmq; do
    cid=$(docker compose -f "${COMPOSE_FILE}" ps -q "${svc}" 2>/dev/null)
    health=$(docker inspect -f '{{.State.Health.Status}}' "${cid}" 2>/dev/null || echo "missing")
    check "TC-health  ${svc} healthy" "$health" "healthy"
done

# в”Җв”Җ TC: dashboard + mailhog phбәЈn hб»“i (khГҙng cГі healthcheck riГӘng, kiб»ғm HTTP trб»ұc tiбәҝp) в”Җв”Җ
dash_code=$(curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" http://localhost:5173/ 2>/dev/null)
check "TC-dashboard  phбәЈn hб»“i HTTP" "$dash_code" "200"
mailhog_code=$(curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" http://localhost:8025/ 2>/dev/null)
check "TC-mailhog  phбәЈn hб»“i HTTP" "$mailhog_code" "200"

# в”Җв”Җ VГІng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt: tбәЎo key вҶ’ tбәЎo rule always-match вҶ’ chб»қ alert THбә¬T tб»ұ trigger в”Җв”Җ
LABEL="smoke-full-$(date +%s)"
create_key=$(curl -s -X POST "${IDENTITY_URL}/api/v1/keys" \
    -H "X-Tenant-Id: ${TENANT_ID}" -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d "{\"label\":\"${LABEL}\"}")
api_key=$(printf '%s' "$create_key" | python3 -c "import sys,json; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get('key',''))" 2>/dev/null)
key_id=$(printf '%s' "$create_key" | python3 -c "import sys,json; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get('id',''))" 2>/dev/null)
check "TC-key  tбәЎo API key qua identity" "$([ -n "$api_key" ] && echo yes || echo no)" "yes"

create_rule=$(curl -s -X POST "${GATEWAY_URL}/api/v1/rules" \
    -H "X-API-Key: ${api_key}" -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"symbol":"BTCUSDT","type":"PRICE_THRESHOLD","params":{"threshold":"1000000","direction":"BELOW"},"webhookUrl":"http://host.docker.internal:9300/hook"}')
rule_status=$(printf '%s' "$create_rule" | python3 -c "import sys,json; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get('status',''))" 2>/dev/null)
rule_id=$(printf '%s' "$create_rule" | python3 -c "import sys,json; print(json.load(sys.stdin).get('id',''))" 2>/dev/null)
check "TC-rule  tбәЎo rule qua gateway (X-API-Key)" "$rule_status" "ACTIVE"

# webhook listener thбәӯt Д‘б»ғ nhбәӯn alert (trade Binance live sбәҪ tб»ұ khб»ӣp ngЖ°б»Ўng cб»ұc cao)
cat > /tmp/smoke-full-webhook.py <<'PYEOF'
import http.server
class Handler(http.server.BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def do_POST(self):
        length = int(self.headers.get("Content-Length", 0))
        self.rfile.read(length)
        self.send_response(200)
        self.end_headers()
    def log_message(self, fmt, *args):
        pass
http.server.HTTPServer(("0.0.0.0", 9300), Handler).serve_forever()
PYEOF
python3 /tmp/smoke-full-webhook.py &
WEBHOOK_PID=$!
sleep 1

echo "      [chб»қ tб»‘i Д‘a ~70s cho trade Binance THбә¬T khб»ӣp ngЖ°б»Ўng вҶ’ alert вҶ’ DELIVERED...]"
alert_status="none"
n=0
while [ "$n" -lt 14 ]; do
    sleep 5; n=$((n + 1))
    alerts=$(curl -s "${GATEWAY_URL}/api/v1/alerts?size=5" -H "X-API-Key: ${api_key}")
    alert_status=$(printf '%s' "$alerts" | python3 -c "
import sys,json
d=json.load(sys.stdin)
content=d.get('content',[])
matching=[a for a in content if a.get('ruleId')=='${rule_id}']
print(matching[0]['status'] if matching else 'none')
" 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
    if [ "$alert_status" = "DELIVERED" ]; then break; fi
done
check "TC-e2e  alert THбә¬T tб»ұ trigger + DELIVERED [+$((n*5))s]" "$alert_status" "DELIVERED"

kill "${WEBHOOK_PID}" 2>/dev/null
rm -f /tmp/smoke-full-webhook.py

# в”Җв”Җ dб»Қn: xoГЎ rule + thu hб»“i key test в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
[ -n "${rule_id}" ] && curl -s -X DELETE "${GATEWAY_URL}/api/v1/rules/${rule_id}" -H "X-API-Key: ${api_key}" >/dev/null 2>&1
[ -n "${key_id}" ] && curl -s -X DELETE "${IDENTITY_URL}/api/v1/keys/${key_id}" -H "X-Tenant-Id: ${TENANT_ID}" >/dev/null 2>&1

echo ""
echo "=== Kбәҝt quбәЈ: PASS=${PASS}  FAIL=${FAIL} ==="
if [ "${FAIL}" -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "PASS  Chбә·ng 10 milestone вҖ” profile full: toГ n bб»ҷ service healthy + luб»“ng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt chбәЎy Д‘бә§u-cuб»‘i"
    exit 0
else
    echo "FAIL  Chбә·ng 10 вҖ” kiб»ғm tra: docker compose -f ${COMPOSE_FILE} logs <service>"
    exit 1
fi

```
Binance WS вҶ’ market-feed вҶ’ TradeEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ
                                            в”ңв”ҖвҶ’ aggregation вҶ’ Candle1mEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ вҶ’ rule-engine
                                            в””в”ҖвҶ’ rule-engine (khi rule match)
                                                    в”Ӯ AlertTriggeredEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ
                                                    в”ңв”ҖвҶ’ alert-delivery вҶ’ POST webhook вҶ’ tenant
                                                    в””в”ҖвҶ’ billing вҶ’ Д‘бәҝm usage вҶ’ quota check
```

## CбәҘu trГәc mono-repo

```
market-pulse/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ common/              # Event DTOs dГ№ng chung (duy nhбәҘt Д‘Ж°б»Јc share giб»Ҝa service)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ gateway/             # Spring Cloud Gateway вҖ” auth + routing
в”ңв”Җв”Җ identity/            # Tenant, Plan, ApiKey CRUD
в”ңв”Җв”Җ market-feed/         # Binance WS client; live/record/replay mode
в”ңв”Җв”Җ aggregation/         # Tumbling 1m window; OHLCV + VWAP
в”ңв”Җв”Җ rule-engine/         # Rule evaluation; quota check
в”ңв”Җв”Җ alert-delivery/      # Webhook delivery + DB-backed retry
в”ңв”Җв”Җ billing/             # Usage counter; quota enforcement
в”ңв”Җв”Җ dashboard/           # React + Vite SPA (NOT Gradle subproject)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ infra/               # docker-compose.yml, .env.example, RabbitMQ definitions
в”ңв”Җв”Җ docs/
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ requirements.md
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ adr/             # ADR-001 вҶ’ ADR-004
в””в”Җв”Җ README.md
```

> **Quy tбәҜc ranh giб»ӣi service:** mб»—i service chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc `implementation(project(":common"))`. KhГҙng import chГ©o giб»Ҝa cГЎc service вҖ” vi phбәЎm lГ  build error. (Xem ADR-002)

## BбәЈng port

| Component | Port | Ghi chГә |
|-----------|------|---------|
| `gateway` | 8080 | Cб»•ng vГ o duy nhбәҘt cho tenant |
| `identity` | 8081 | Internal + qua gateway |
| `market-feed` | 8082 | KhГҙng expose REST ra ngoГ i |
| `rule-engine` | 8083 | Qua gateway |
| `alert-delivery` | 8084 | Qua gateway |
| `billing` | 8085 | Qua gateway + internal |
| `aggregation` | 8086 | Internal only |
| `dashboard` | 5173 | Dev: Vite dev server В· Docker (`--profile full`): build tД©nh phб»Ҙc vб»Ҙ qua Caddy |
| `identity-db` (PG) | 5432 | |
| `aggregation-db` (PG) | 5433 | |
| `rule-engine-db` (PG) | 5434 | |
| `alert-delivery-db` (PG) | 5435 | |
| `billing-db` (PG) | 5436 | |

| RabbitMQ Management UI | 15672 | `guest/guest` |
| Mailhog SMTP | 1025 | |
| Mailhog Web UI | 8025 | |

## Compose profile

Mб»—i profile nhГіm cГЎc service liГӘn quan вҖ” khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng tб»«ng phбә§n mГ  khГҙng cбә§n bбәӯt toГ n bб»ҷ JVM tб»« Chбә·ng 1.

| Profile | Service khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng | Mб»Ҙc Д‘Гӯch |
|---------|-------------------|---------|
| `core` | gateway, identity, identity-db | Auth + routing вҖ” Chбә·ng 2 |
| `feed` | market-feed, rabbitmq | DГІng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Binance вҖ” Chбә·ng 3 |
| `processing` | aggregation, aggregation-db, rule-engine, rule-engine-db, rabbitmq | Aggregation + rule eval вҖ” Chбә·ng 4вҖ“5 |
| `delivery` | alert-delivery, alert-delivery-db, billing, billing-db, mailhog, rabbitmq | Delivery + billing вҖ” Chбә·ng 6вҖ“7 |
| `full` | tбәҘt cбәЈ + dashboard | End-to-end вҖ” Chбә·ng 8вҖ“10 |

> **LЖ°u ГҪ:** CГЎc profile trГӘn sбәҪ hoГ n thiб»Үn dбә§n theo chбә·ng. б»һ Chбә·ng 1, file `docker-compose.yml` chЖ°a tб»“n tбәЎi вҖ” Д‘Ж°б»Јc build tб»« Chбә·ng 2 trб»ҹ Д‘i.

```bash
# VГӯ dб»Ҙ chбәЎy profile core (Chбә·ng 2 trб»ҹ Д‘i)
docker compose --profile core up -d

# Kiб»ғm tra health
docker compose ps

# Xem log service cб»Ҙ thб»ғ
docker compose logs -f gateway

# Dб»«ng
docker compose --profile core down
```

---

## Prerequisite

- Docker Desktop вүҘ 4.x (Engine вүҘ 24)
- Java 21 (Temurin/GraalVM CE)
- Gradle 8.x (wrapper tб»ұ tбәЈi вҖ” khГҙng cбә§n cГ i tay)
- Node.js 20 (chб»ү cбә§n cho `dashboard/`; `package-lock.json` Д‘ГЈ ghim `vite@6`/`plugin-react@4` vГ¬
  Vite 8 mб»ӣi nhбәҘt Д‘ГІi Node 20.19+ вҖ” `npm ci` tГЎi lбәӯp Д‘Гәng bбәЈn bбәҘt kб»ғ patch version Node cГ i local)
- RAM tб»‘i thiб»ғu: 16 GB (profile `full` ~3.5вҖ“4.2 GB)

---

## Quick Start вҖ” chбәЎy toГ n bб»ҷ hб»Ү tб»« Д‘бә§u

```bash
cd infra
cp .env.example .env   # Д‘iб»Ғn mбәӯt khбә©u thбәӯt nбәҝu cбә§n, mбә·c Д‘б»Ӣnh "change_me" Д‘б»§ dГ№ng local

# Build + chбәЎy TOГҖN Bб»ҳ (7 JVM + 5 Postgres + RabbitMQ + Mailhog + Dashboard)
docker compose --env-file .env --profile full up -d --build

# Verify mб»Қi service healthy + 1 vГІng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt (tбәЎo rule вҶ’ trade Binance live вҶ’ DELIVERED)
cd .. && bash scripts/smoke-full.sh
```

**TбәЎo API key Д‘бә§u tiГӘn** (bootstrap вҖ” gб»Қi thбәіng `identity`, KHГ”NG qua gateway vГ¬ cбә§n `X-Tenant-Id`
trЖ°б»ӣc khi cГі key; cГЎc thao tГЎc SAU Д‘Гі вҖ” kб»ғ cбәЈ tбәЎo thГӘm key вҖ” Д‘б»Ғu qua gateway vб»ӣi `X-API-Key`):

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:8081/api/v1/keys \
  -H "X-Tenant-Id: 00000000-0000-0000-0001-000000000001" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{"label":"my-first-key"}'
```

Hoбә·c dГ№ng luГҙn key demo cГі sбәөn (seed `V2__seed.sql`, tenant "Acme Corp", gГіi `starter`):
`demo-key-acme-2026` вҖ” dГЎn vГ o mГ n Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp dashboard tбәЎi http://localhost:5173.

## Scripts kiб»ғm thб»ӯ tham khбәЈo

| Script | Kiб»ғm gГ¬ |
|--------|---------|
| `scripts/smoke-ch2.sh` вҖҰ `smoke-ch7.sh` | Milestone tб»«ng chбә·ng riГӘng lбә» (gateway/identity, market-feed, aggregation, rule-engine, alert-delivery, billing) |
| `scripts/smoke-full.sh` | Milestone Chбә·ng 10 вҖ” toГ n bб»ҷ `--profile full` healthy + 1 vГІng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt Д‘бә§u-cuб»‘i |
| `scripts/load-test.sh <multiplier> [giГўy] [file]` | Chбә·ng 9 вҖ” replay б»ҹ tб»‘c Д‘б»ҷ bбәҘt kб»і, theo dГөi queue depth `rule-engine.trades` so ngЖ°б»Ўng gГЈy (>5,000 msg, xem [docs/load-test-report.md](docs/load-test-report.md)) |

## Tham khбәЈo

- [docs/requirements.md](docs/requirements.md) вҖ” Product requirements
- [docs/adr/](docs/adr/) вҖ” Architecture Decision Records
- [docs/load-test-report.md](docs/load-test-report.md) вҖ” Chбә·ng 9: kбәҝt quбәЈ load-test thбәӯt (dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Binance thбәӯt, khГҙng dб»ұng sб»‘)
- Lab content: xem trГӘn nб»Ғn tбәЈng Praxis
64:T2b67,# Market Pulse

Nб»Ғn tбәЈng cбәЈnh bГЎo thб»Ӣ trЖ°б»қng real-time theo mГҙ hГ¬nh B2B. Tenant Д‘Дғng kГҪ rule (ngЖ°б»Ўng giГЎ, thay Д‘б»•i %, Д‘б»ҷt biбәҝn volume), khi Д‘iб»Ғu kiб»Үn khб»ӣp hб»Ү tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng gб»Қi webhook. Dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Д‘бәҝn tб»« Binance WebSocket (~80 trades/giГўy vб»ӣi BTC/USDT).

**Mб»Ҙc Д‘Гӯch:** ДҗГўy lГ  repo mбә«u cho Lab lб»ӣn trГӘn nб»Ғn tбәЈng Praxis вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc xГўy tб»«ng bЖ°б»ӣc theo 10 chбә·ng, mб»—i chбә·ng kбәҝt thГәc bбәұng milestone cГі thб»ғ chбәЎy thбәӯt.
