**Luб»“ng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu chГӯnh:**

```
Binance WS вҶ’ market-feed вҶ’ TradeEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ
                                            в”ңв”ҖвҶ’ aggregation вҶ’ Candle1mEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ вҶ’ rule-engine
                                            в””в”ҖвҶ’ rule-engine (khi rule match)
                                                    в”Ӯ AlertTriggeredEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ
                                                    в”ңв”ҖвҶ’ alert-delivery вҶ’ POST webhook вҶ’ tenant
                                                    в””в”ҖвҶ’ billing вҶ’ Д‘бәҝm usage вҶ’ quota check
```

---

## CбәҘu trГәc mono-repo

```
market-pulse/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ common/              # Event DTOs dГ№ng chung (duy nhбәҘt Д‘Ж°б»Јc share giб»Ҝa service)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ gateway/             # Spring Cloud Gateway вҖ” auth + routing
в”ңв”Җв”Җ identity/            # Tenant, Plan, ApiKey CRUD
в”ңв”Җв”Җ market-feed/         # Binance WS client; live/record/replay mode
в”ңв”Җв”Җ aggregation/         # Tumbling 1m window; OHLCV + VWAP
в”ңв”Җв”Җ rule-engine/         # Rule evaluation; quota check
в”ңв”Җв”Җ alert-delivery/      # Webhook delivery + DB-backed retry
в”ңв”Җв”Җ billing/             # Usage counter; quota enforcement
в”ңв”Җв”Җ dashboard/           # React + Vite SPA (NOT Gradle subproject)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ infra/               # docker-compose.yml, .env.example, RabbitMQ definitions
в”ңв”Җв”Җ docs/
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ requirements.md
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ adr/             # ADR-001 вҶ’ ADR-004
в””в”Җв”Җ README.md
```

> **Quy tбәҜc ranh giб»ӣi service:** mб»—i service chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc `implementation(project(":common"))`. KhГҙng import chГ©o giб»Ҝa cГЎc service вҖ” vi phбәЎm lГ  build error. (Xem ADR-002)

```bash
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{"label":"my-first-key"}'
```

Hoбә·c dГ№ng luГҙn key demo cГі sбәөn (seed `V2__seed.sql`, tenant "Acme Corp", gГіi `starter`):
`demo-key-acme-2026` вҖ” dГЎn vГ o mГ n Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp dashboard tбәЎi http://localhost:5173.

## Scripts kiб»ғm thб»ӯ tham khбәЈo

| Script | Kiб»ғm gГ¬ |
|--------|---------|
| `scripts/smoke-ch2.sh` вҖҰ `smoke-ch7.sh` | Milestone tб»«ng chбә·ng riГӘng lбә» (gateway/identity, market-feed, aggregation, rule-engine, alert-delivery, billing) |
| `scripts/smoke-full.sh` | Milestone Chбә·ng 10 вҖ” toГ n bб»ҷ `--profile full` healthy + 1 vГІng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt Д‘бә§u-cuб»‘i |
| `scripts/load-test.sh <multiplier> [giГўy] [file]` | Chбә·ng 9 вҖ” replay б»ҹ tб»‘c Д‘б»ҷ bбәҘt kб»і, theo dГөi queue depth `rule-engine.trades` so ngЖ°б»Ўng gГЈy (>5,000 msg, xem [docs/load-test-report.md](docs/load-test-report.md)) |

---

## Backup & Restore

Mб»—i Postgres dГ№ng Docker named volume (`identity-db-data`, `aggregation-db-data`, ...) вҖ” restart
container khГҙng mбәҘt dб»Ҝ liб»Үu; Flyway tб»ұ chбәЎy lбәЎi migration khi khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng (idempotent, chб»ү ГЎp version
mб»ӣi). ДҗГЈ verify thбәӯt `pg_dump` вҶ’ restore vГ o Postgres tбәЎm khГҙi phб»Ҙc Д‘Гәng 100% dб»Ҝ liб»Үu:

```bash
docker exec infra-identity-db-1 pg_dump -U identity_user -d identity --clean --if-exists > backup.sql
# khГҙi phб»Ҙc (vГ o DB mб»ӣi hoбә·c DB cЕ© sau khi mбәҘt dб»Ҝ liб»Үu):
docker exec -i <container-db-Д‘Гӯch> psql -U identity_user -d identity < backup.sql
```

74:T28f3,# Market Pulse

Nб»Ғn tбәЈng cбәЈnh bГЎo thб»Ӣ trЖ°б»қng real-time theo mГҙ hГ¬nh B2B. Tenant Д‘Дғng kГҪ rule (ngЖ°б»Ўng giГЎ, thay Д‘б»•i %, Д‘б»ҷt biбәҝn volume), khi Д‘iб»Ғu kiб»Үn khб»ӣp hб»Ү tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng gб»Қi webhook. Dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Д‘бәҝn tб»« Binance WebSocket (~80 trades/giГўy vб»ӣi BTC/USDT).

**Mб»Ҙc Д‘Гӯch:** ДҗГўy lГ  repo mбә«u cho Lab lб»ӣn trГӘn nб»Ғn tбәЈng Praxis вҖ” ngЖ°б»қi hб»Қc xГўy tб»«ng bЖ°б»ӣc theo 10 chбә·ng, mб»—i chбә·ng kбәҝt thГәc bбәұng milestone cГі thб»ғ chбәЎy thбәӯt.

---

**Luб»“ng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu chГӯnh:**

```
Binance WS вҶ’ market-feed вҶ’ TradeEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ
                                            в”ңв”ҖвҶ’ aggregation вҶ’ Candle1mEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ вҶ’ rule-engine
                                            в””в”ҖвҶ’ rule-engine (khi rule match)
                                                    в”Ӯ AlertTriggeredEvent вҶ’ RabbitMQ
                                                    в”ңв”ҖвҶ’ alert-delivery вҶ’ POST webhook вҶ’ tenant
                                                    в””в”ҖвҶ’ billing вҶ’ Д‘бәҝm usage вҶ’ quota check
```

---

## CбәҘu trГәc mono-repo

```
market-pulse/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ common/              # Event DTOs dГ№ng chung (duy nhбәҘt Д‘Ж°б»Јc share giб»Ҝa service)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ gateway/             # Spring Cloud Gateway вҖ” auth + routing
в”ңв”Җв”Җ identity/            # Tenant, Plan, ApiKey CRUD
в”ңв”Җв”Җ market-feed/         # Binance WS client; live/record/replay mode
в”ңв”Җв”Җ aggregation/         # Tumbling 1m window; OHLCV + VWAP
в”ңв”Җв”Җ rule-engine/         # Rule evaluation; quota check
в”ңв”Җв”Җ alert-delivery/      # Webhook delivery + DB-backed retry
в”ңв”Җв”Җ billing/             # Usage counter; quota enforcement
в”ңв”Җв”Җ dashboard/           # React + Vite SPA (NOT Gradle subproject)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ infra/               # docker-compose.yml, .env.example, RabbitMQ definitions
в”ңв”Җв”Җ docs/
в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ requirements.md
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ adr/             # ADR-001 вҶ’ ADR-004
в””в”Җв”Җ README.md
```

> **Quy tбәҜc ranh giб»ӣi service:** mб»—i service chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc `implementation(project(":common"))`. KhГҙng import chГ©o giб»Ҝa cГЎc service вҖ” vi phбәЎm lГ  build error. (Xem ADR-002)

---

## Compose profile

Mб»—i profile nhГіm cГЎc service liГӘn quan вҖ” khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng tб»«ng phбә§n mГ  khГҙng cбә§n bбәӯt toГ n bб»ҷ JVM tб»« Chбә·ng 1.

| Profile | Service khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng | Mб»Ҙc Д‘Гӯch |
|---------|-------------------|---------|
| `core` | gateway, identity, identity-db | Auth + routing вҖ” Chбә·ng 2 |
| `feed` | market-feed, rabbitmq | DГІng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Binance вҖ” Chбә·ng 3 |
| `processing` | aggregation, aggregation-db, rule-engine, rule-engine-db, rabbitmq | Aggregation + rule eval вҖ” Chбә·ng 4вҖ“5 |
| `delivery` | alert-delivery, alert-delivery-db, billing, billing-db, mailhog, rabbitmq | Delivery + billing вҖ” Chбә·ng 6вҖ“7 |
| `full` | tбәҘt cбәЈ + dashboard | End-to-end вҖ” Chбә·ng 8вҖ“10 |

> **LЖ°u ГҪ:** CГЎc profile trГӘn sбәҪ hoГ n thiб»Үn dбә§n theo chбә·ng. б»һ Chбә·ng 1, file `docker-compose.yml` chЖ°a tб»“n tбәЎi вҖ” Д‘Ж°б»Јc build tб»« Chбә·ng 2 trб»ҹ Д‘i.

```bash
# VГӯ dб»Ҙ chбәЎy profile core (Chбә·ng 2 trб»ҹ Д‘i)
docker compose --profile core up -d

# Kiб»ғm tra health
docker compose ps

# Xem log service cб»Ҙ thб»ғ
docker compose logs -f gateway

# Dб»«ng
docker compose --profile core down
```

---

## Prerequisite

- Docker Desktop вүҘ 4.x (Engine вүҘ 24)
- Java 21 (Temurin/GraalVM CE)
- Gradle 8.x (wrapper tб»ұ tбәЈi вҖ” khГҙng cбә§n cГ i tay)
- Node.js 20 (chб»ү cбә§n cho `dashboard/`; `package-lock.json` Д‘ГЈ ghim `vite@6`/`plugin-react@4` vГ¬
  Vite 8 mб»ӣi nhбәҘt Д‘ГІi Node 20.19+ вҖ” `npm ci` tГЎi lбәӯp Д‘Гәng bбәЈn bбәҘt kб»ғ patch version Node cГ i local)
- RAM tб»‘i thiб»ғu: 16 GB (profile `full` ~3.5вҖ“4.2 GB)

---

## Quick Start вҖ” chбәЎy toГ n bб»ҷ hб»Ү tб»« Д‘бә§u

```bash
cd infra
cp .env.example .env   # Д‘iб»Ғn mбәӯt khбә©u thбәӯt nбәҝu cбә§n, mбә·c Д‘б»Ӣnh "change_me" Д‘б»§ dГ№ng local

# Build + chбәЎy TOГҖN Bб»ҳ (7 JVM + 5 Postgres + RabbitMQ + Mailhog + Dashboard)
docker compose --env-file .env --profile full up -d --build

# Verify mб»Қi service healthy + 1 vГІng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt (tбәЎo rule вҶ’ trade Binance live вҶ’ DELIVERED)
cd .. && bash scripts/smoke-full.sh
```

**TбәЎo API key Д‘бә§u tiГӘn** (bootstrap вҖ” gб»Қi thбәіng `identity`, KHГ”NG qua gateway vГ¬ cбә§n `X-Tenant-Id`
trЖ°б»ӣc khi cГі key; cГЎc thao tГЎc SAU Д‘Гі вҖ” kб»ғ cбәЈ tбәЎo thГӘm key вҖ” Д‘б»Ғu qua gateway vб»ӣi `X-API-Key`):

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:8081/api/v1/keys \
  -H "X-Tenant-Id: 00000000-0000-0000-0001-000000000001" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d '{"label":"my-first-key"}'
```

Hoбә·c dГ№ng luГҙn key demo cГі sбәөn (seed `V2__seed.sql`, tenant "Acme Corp", gГіi `starter`):
`demo-key-acme-2026` вҖ” dГЎn vГ o mГ n Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp dashboard tбәЎi http://localhost:5173.

## Scripts kiб»ғm thб»ӯ tham khбәЈo

| Script | Kiб»ғm gГ¬ |
|--------|---------|
| `scripts/smoke-ch2.sh` вҖҰ `smoke-ch7.sh` | Milestone tб»«ng chбә·ng riГӘng lбә» (gateway/identity, market-feed, aggregation, rule-engine, alert-delivery, billing) |
| `scripts/smoke-full.sh` | Milestone Chбә·ng 10 вҖ” toГ n bб»ҷ `--profile full` healthy + 1 vГІng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt Д‘бә§u-cuб»‘i |
| `scripts/load-test.sh <multiplier> [giГўy] [file]` | Chбә·ng 9 вҖ” replay б»ҹ tб»‘c Д‘б»ҷ bбәҘt kб»і, theo dГөi queue depth `rule-engine.trades` so ngЖ°б»Ўng gГЈy (>5,000 msg, xem [docs/load-test-report.md](docs/load-test-report.md)) |

<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF;font-weight:bold">## CбәҘu trГәc mono-repo</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">```</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">market-pulse/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ common/              # Event DTOs dГ№ng chung (duy nhбәҘt Д‘Ж°б»Јc share giб»Ҝa service)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ gateway/             # Spring Cloud Gateway вҖ” auth + routing</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ identity/            # Tenant, Plan, ApiKey CRUD</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ market-feed/         # Binance WS client; live/record/replay mode</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ aggregation/         # Tumbling 1m window; OHLCV + VWAP</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ rule-engine/         # Rule evaluation; quota check</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ alert-delivery/      # Webhook delivery + DB-backed retry</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ billing/             # Usage counter; quota enforcement</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ dashboard/           # React + Vite SPA (NOT Gradle subproject)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ infra/               # docker-compose.yml, .env.example, RabbitMQ definitions</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”ңв”Җв”Җ docs/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ requirements.md</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ adr/             # ADR-001 вҶ’ ADR-004</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">в””в”Җв”Җ README.md</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">```</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#7EE787">> </span><span style="color:#E6EDF3;font-weight:bold">**Quy tбәҜc ranh giб»ӣi service:**</span><span style="color:#7EE787"> mб»—i service chб»ү Д‘Ж°б»Јc </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`implementation(project(":common"))`</span><span style="color:#7EE787">. KhГҙng import chГ©o giб»Ҝa cГЎc service вҖ” vi phбәЎm lГ  build error. (Xem ADR-002)</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF;font-weight:bold">## BбәЈng port</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">| Component | Port | Ghi chГә |</span></span>

<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF;font-weight:bold">## Compose profile</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">Mб»—i profile nhГіm cГЎc service liГӘn quan вҖ” khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng tб»«ng phбә§n mГ  khГҙng cбә§n bбәӯt toГ n bб»ҷ JVM tб»« Chбә·ng 1.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">| Profile | Service khб»ҹi Д‘б»ҷng | Mб»Ҙc Д‘Гӯch |</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">|---------|-------------------|---------|</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">| </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`core`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> | gateway, identity, identity-db | Auth + routing вҖ” Chбә·ng 2 |</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">| </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`feed`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> | market-feed, rabbitmq | DГІng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Binance вҖ” Chбә·ng 3 |</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">| </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`processing`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> | aggregation, aggregation-db, rule-engine, rule-engine-db, rabbitmq | Aggregation + rule eval вҖ” Chбә·ng 4вҖ“5 |</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">| </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`delivery`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> | alert-delivery, alert-delivery-db, billing, billing-db, mailhog, rabbitmq | Delivery + billing вҖ” Chбә·ng 6вҖ“7 |</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">| </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`full`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> | tбәҘt cбәЈ + dashboard | End-to-end вҖ” Chбә·ng 8вҖ“10 |</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7EE787">> </span><span style="color:#E6EDF3;font-weight:bold">**LЖ°u ГҪ:**</span><span style="color:#7EE787"> CГЎc profile trГӘn sбәҪ hoГ n thiб»Үn dбә§n theo chбә·ng. б»һ Chбә·ng 1, file </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`docker-compose.yml`</span><span style="color:#7EE787"> chЖ°a tб»“n tбәЎi вҖ” Д‘Ж°б»Јc build tб»« Chбә·ng 2 trб»ҹ Д‘i.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E"># VГӯ dб»Ҙ chбәЎy profile core (Chбә·ng 2 trб»ҹ Д‘i)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">docker</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> compose</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> --profile</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> core</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> up</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> -d</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E"># Kiб»ғm tra health</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">docker</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> compose</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> ps</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E"># Xem log service cб»Ҙ thб»ғ</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">docker</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> compose</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> logs</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> -f</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> gateway</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E"># Dб»«ng</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">docker</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> compose</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> --profile</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> core</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> down</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF;font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF;font-weight:bold">## Prerequisite</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">-</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> Docker Desktop вүҘ 4.x (Engine вүҘ 24)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">-</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> Java 21 (Temurin/GraalVM CE)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">-</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> Gradle 8.x (wrapper tб»ұ tбәЈi вҖ” khГҙng cбә§n cГ i tay)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">-</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> Node.js 20 (chб»ү cбә§n cho </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`dashboard/`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">; </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`package-lock.json`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> Д‘ГЈ ghim </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`vite@6`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">/</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`plugin-react@4`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> vГ¬</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  Vite 8 mб»ӣi nhбәҘt Д‘ГІi Node 20.19+ вҖ” </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`npm ci`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tГЎi lбәӯp Д‘Гәng bбәЈn bбәҘt kб»ғ patch version Node cГ i local)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">-</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> RAM tб»‘i thiб»ғu: 16 GB (profile </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`full`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> ~3.5вҖ“4.2 GB)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF;font-weight:bold">---</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF;font-weight:bold">## Quick Start вҖ” chбәЎy toГ n bб»ҷ hб»Ү tб»« Д‘бә§u</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">cd</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> infra</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">cp</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> .env.example</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> .env</span><span style="color:#8B949E">   # Д‘iб»Ғn mбәӯt khбә©u thбәӯt nбәҝu cбә§n, mбә·c Д‘б»Ӣnh "change_me" Д‘б»§ dГ№ng local</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E"># Build + chбәЎy TOГҖN Bб»ҳ (7 JVM + 5 Postgres + RabbitMQ + Mailhog + Dashboard)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">docker</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> compose</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> --env-file</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> .env</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> --profile</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> full</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> up</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> -d</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> --build</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E"># Verify mб»Қi service healthy + 1 vГІng nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ thбәӯt (tбәЎo rule вҶ’ trade Binance live вҶ’ DELIVERED)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">cd</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> ..</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> &#x26;&#x26; </span><span style="color:#FFA657">bash</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> scripts/smoke-full.sh</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3;font-weight:bold">**TбәЎo API key Д‘бә§u tiГӘn**</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (bootstrap вҖ” gб»Қi thбәіng </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`identity`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, KHГ”NG qua gateway vГ¬ cбә§n </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`X-Tenant-Id`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">trЖ°б»ӣc khi cГі key; cГЎc thao tГЎc SAU Д‘Гі вҖ” kб»ғ cбәЈ tбәЎo thГӘm key вҖ” Д‘б»Ғu qua gateway vб»ӣi </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`X-API-Key`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">):</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">```bash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">curl</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> -X</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> POST</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> http://localhost:8081/api/v1/keys</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> \</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  -H "X-Tenant-Id: 00000000-0000-0000-0001-000000000001" \</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  -H</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> "Content-Type: application/json"</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> -d</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> '{"label":"my-first-key"}'</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">```</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">Hoбә·c dГ№ng luГҙn key demo cГі sбәөn (seed </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`V2__seed.sql`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, tenant "Acme Corp", gГіi </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">`starter`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">`demo-key-acme-2026`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> вҖ” dГЎn vГ o mГ n Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp dashboard tбәЎi http://localhost:5173.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
